Second Regular Meeting of the National Government 65

Addition of Embassies in Poland and Czechoslovakia

Bereavement Expenses for Xie Guoliang and Xie Shu

Regulations for the Panchen Lama's Annual Salary and Official Expenses

On the morning of the 3rd, the National Government held its second regular meeting. The attending committee members were Wang Zhengting, Shao Yuanchong, Wang Boqun, Zhu Peide, Yu Youren, Dai Chuanxian, Chen Guofu, Liu Shangqing, Ding Weifen, Kong Xiangxi, Ye Chucang, Ma Fuxiang, and Shao Lizi. Yu Youren chaired the meeting. The matters discussed included: (1) The Executive Yuan submitted a request from the Ministry of Foreign Affairs to establish embassies in Poland and Czechoslovakia and to appoint the minister to Poland concurrently as the minister to Czechoslovakia. The question of whether this should be submitted for approval was discussed. The decision was made to proceed according to the resolution of the 28th State Council meeting of the Executive Yuan and to submit the proposal for review and implementation. (2) It was decided to announce the revised temporary measures for auditing Chilean nitrate. (3) The Executive Yuan submitted a request from the Mongolian and Tibetan Affairs Commission stating that Xie Guoliang, a former specialist of the commission, was dispatched to Tibet, accompanied by his son, Xie Shu, as his secretary. Unfortunately, they died of illness en route. It was proposed that Xie Guoliang be treated as a simplified-appointment official and his son Xie Shu as a recommended-appointment official, with bereavement payments and one-time condolence payments given to their families to encourage others. Additionally, it was requested that Xie Guoliang be given 3,000 yuan in bereavement expenses and Xie Shu 2,000 yuan. The decision was to grant 5,000 yuan in bereavement expenses, and the bereavement payments and one-time condolence payments for their families were to be handled by the Examination Yuan. (4) It was decided to announce the revised organization regulations for ordnance factories. (5) It was decided to announce the revised articles 20 to 24 of the organizational law of the Ministry of Education. (6) It was decided to announce the revised articles 12 to 16 and 18 of the organizational law of the Capital Police Department. (7) It was decided to announce the revised article 11 of the short-term public bond regulations for dredging the Hai River project in Hebei Province. (8) The Examination Yuan submitted that the regulations for the screening and review of incumbent civil servants still needed to be extended. It was proposed to announce the extension of the regulations for the screening and review of incumbent civil servants for recommended-appointment and higher-level personnel by three months until the end of September of this year, and for assigned-appointment personnel by six months until the end of December of this year. The decision was to extend the deadline for all categories to the end of December of this year. (9) It was decided to appoint Wu Jianchang as a councilor of the Control Yuan. (10) It was decided to appoint Gu Zhutong as the commander of the Guard Army and concurrently as the commander of the First Division of the army. (11) It was decided to appoint Wang Taiqi, Wang Zhenbang, Liu Zanzhou, Lin Zhuo, Wang Renpei, Ma Fangzheng, Song Banghan, Wu Wenfu, Wang Richang, Liu Haishan, and Ma Zhentai as colonels on the advisory board of the Military Council. (12) The Chief of Accounting, Chen Qicai, proposed the "Provisional Regulations for Budgeting, Accounting, and Statistics Personnel in Various Agencies" of the National Government's Directorate General of Budgets, Accounting and Statistics for review. The decision was to approve and announce the regulations. (13) It was decided to announce the "Regulations for Rewards and Punishments of Administrative Personnel at All Levels During the Bandit Suppression Period." (14) It was decided that the annual salary of the Grand Master Guanghui would be 120,000 yuan, to be paid monthly by the central government. His personal expenses and the living expenses of his accompanying monks would be paid from this salary. In addition to the annual salary, a monthly allowance of 30,000 yuan would be provided by the central government for official expenses. All hospitality expenses would be discontinued. (15) It was decided to additionally appoint Zhang Zhijiang as a member of the Preparatory Committee for the National Games of the 20th year of the Republic of China.

Changes After the Sino-Russian Conference 66

Russia Proposes Abolishing the Board of Directors and Supervisory Board and Increasing the Authority of the Director-General

The Issue of Road Redemption Will Be Discussed Based on Previously Agreed Principles

Mo Dehui Presents Four Counter-Proposals – Harbin Correspondence: Since the seventh meeting, the Sino-Soviet conference has shifted its focus from the issue of road redemption to changes in the current system of the Chinese Eastern Railway (CER). However, at the eighth meeting, Karakhan proposed changing the CER's management rules, increasing the authority of the director-general, and abolishing the railway board of directors. A fierce debate erupted during the meeting, and no resolution was reached. The eighth meeting was originally scheduled for June 16, but Karakhan suddenly claimed he had to host a diplomatic corps that day and requested a postponement. The eighth meeting took place on June 21. According to the official gazette published by the Moscow delegation, only a few words were mentioned, simply stating that the meeting took place as scheduled. The ninth meeting was convened on June 24. The official news received still stopped there. Whether there were disputes in the two meetings and how the negotiations on the road redemption issue ended remained unmentioned. The Liaoning National Diplomacy Association believed that the diplomatic situation was changing so drastically during this tense meeting that, although Mo Dehui did not report to Shenyang, the external affairs department should have received telegrams. The people of the Northeast were most concerned about the Sino-Soviet conference, so they telegraphed Beijing a few days ago, requesting a detailed response from the external affairs department so that it could be conveyed to the public. According to a fast letter from Moscow on the 24th obtained from a certain party here, the truth of the meeting was that the representatives of both sides agreed at the eighth meeting to temporarily suspend discussions on the road redemption issue. All previously agreed matters would be handed over to the plenipotentiary representatives of both sides for signing after special committees had organized them, and this would serve as the principle for future discussions. Mo Dehui immediately proposed counter-proposals to Karakhan's proposal to change the current rules of the CER and abolish the board of directors, which were divided into four items: (1) changes to the organization of the CER administration; (2) equal employment of Chinese and Russian personnel; (3) equal deposit of railway funds in Chinese and Russian banks; and (4) simultaneous use of Chinese and Russian languages. These items had not been resolved by the CER board of directors over the years and had become disputes, or even if they had been resolved, there were still problems. The Russian plenipotentiary did not agree with these counter-proposals and responded item by item when the ninth meeting was convened, refuting almost everything. Their claim was still that the CER's business was declining, and its income was insufficient to maintain operations. Abolishing the board of directors and supervisory board would reduce disputes and save money. They argued that the director-general's authority was increased in name only and was still subject to the supervision of the Chinese superintendent. Important matters were still decided by meetings, only merging the powers of the board of directors and supervisory board into the railway administration. Senior Chinese officials still had the right to speak and make suggestions. Mo Dehui replied that the CER was a Sino-Russian joint venture, and the board of directors was a legislative body. All railway regulations originated from it. The railway administration was an executive body. The board of directors was like the shareholders, and the director-general was the hired manager. Without a board of directors, the company would have no shareholders. If the manager acted arbitrarily and held great power, who could come out to restrain them when things got out of hand, and who would have the right to restrain them? Karakhan also refuted Mo with sophistry. How things will proceed in the future will have to wait for the tenth meeting to discuss. The current system of the CER is based on the organization of the Fengtian-Russian and Sino-Russian internal agreements. However, only 40 to 50 percent of what is contained in the agreement has been realized. For example, equal employment and the simultaneous use of Chinese and Russian languages were stipulated early in the agreement, but they have not been realized in practice. This time, Russia's proposal to change the management rules is intended to overturn the Fengtian-Russian and Sino-Russian agreements, and their intention is very dangerous. It goes without saying. The Russian side has always had a strong influence on the management rules and the director-general's authority of the CER. How did the CER war of the 18th year of the Republic of China start? The Chinese people have not forgotten it. Since the signing of the Khabarovsk Record, Russia has used the remaining power of the victor to manipulate railway affairs with its great power, disregard the Chinese side, and act arbitrarily, even more so than before. The Chinese staff serving in the railway, for the sake of keeping their rubles and their positions, competed to make concessions in everything, taking irresponsibility and avoiding Russian dissatisfaction as virtues. As a result, Russian influence increased day by day, while the status of Chinese staff decreased. "Checking in and receiving salary" is a common term used by Russian staff to describe the Chinese side. Without fundamentally improving the organizational and management laws, the power of the Chinese side will become increasingly threatened. We deeply hope that the Russian meeting will discuss this matter. However, the starting points are the same, but the destinations are different. What we earnestly hope for is the full implementation of the Sino-Russian and Fengtian-Russian agreements. What Russia hopes for is to overturn the agreements, abolish the board of directors and supervisory board, and increase the power of the director-general. The prices are vastly different, so it is clear that a conclusion cannot be reached in a short period of time. (29th)

Victory in the Suppression of Communists by Various Divisions and Brigades in Fujian 67

Customs Collects Bandit Suppression Fees on Behalf

筹Building an Aircraft Field for Bandit Suppression

Fuzhou Correspondence: Regarding the suppression of communists in the upper reaches, Division Commander Liu Heding, in his capacity as the Bandit Suppression Commander of Fujian Province, has led his direct troops and the units under his command to launch attacks on the counties invaded by communist bandits. At the same time, he is also building trenches in the areas of Shunchang, Yangkou, and Yanping to block the bandits. According to daily reports, the bandits in Jiangle, after being suppressed twice by Zhou Zhiqin in Guangming and Shuiji, mostly fled north. Although there are a few remaining bandits in Jianning and Shouning counties that have not retreated, Lin Pingzhou and Qian Yuguang's brigades are being strictly ordered to scout and suppress them. As for the Shaoguang area, the vanguard of Division Commander Liu's troops had already passed Dagan on the 22nd and was advancing towards Shaowu County, and it is estimated that they can reach Changting and Ninghua, etc. Lu's troops have also sent teams to assist in the defense. The provincial government received a telegram from Lu Xinming yesterday, stating that Changting was once invaded by the defeated bandits of Ruijin on the day of Xiaori. Upon hearing the news, the troops returned from Shicheng on Qiaori and fought back bravely. They recovered Changting at noon that day, etc. It can be seen that the communist scourge in northern and western Fujian will soon be quelled.

Regarding the bandit suppression fees, the provincial government previously planned carefully. On the 28th of this month, a special temporary meeting was held. In addition to the measures for establishing the Provincial Prohibited-Smoking Investigation Office, the provincial government wired the central government for interpretation based on the requests from all sectors. (1) The proposal to collect one month's rent from the entire province was decided to be implemented as planned to meet military needs. It is expected to start collecting in early next month. (2) The proposal to have the Fuzhou, Xiamen, and Sandu customs collect bandit suppression fees on behalf was decided to be handed over to the Military Needs Design Committee for proper planning. In Xiamen, the Provincial Steering Committee Chen Lianfang and the two committee members Hong Xiaochun and Chen Ruiqing have negotiated and are now consulting with the tax authorities. In addition, the provincial government and Division Commander Liu believe that aircraft is very important for military operations, and have telegraphed the central government to quickly allocate several seaplanes to the province for use. It is heard that the central government has ordered the Aviation Administration to send Lin Jiatan to Fujian to negotiate the construction of the aircraft field. Lin arrived in the province on the 28th and went to the provincial government at 10:00 a.m. to meet with the committee members to discuss everything. It is heard that this aircraft field is planned to be set up in five locations: one in Fuzhou, two in Funing, three in Longxi, four in Jinjiang, and five in Yanping. (June 30)

Severe Flooding in Fuzhou 68

Public Buses Suspended – Boats Used in Upper Streets

Many Residents Drowned – Countless Houses Collapsed

Foul Odor May Cause Epidemic – Local Authorities Preparing for Emergency Relief

Fuzhou Correspondence: Since mid-June, Fujian has been plagued by continuous rain, and the rivers have overflowed. On the evening of the 23rd, mountain torrents in the upper reaches of the Min River suddenly surged and rushed down, and by the morning of the 24th, low-lying areas in the city were submerged. After the afternoon, the floodwaters rose higher and higher, and by about 10:00 p.m., the entire city, except for the northeast corners, had become a swamp. According to a report from the Municipal Public Security Bureau, the depth of the floodwaters at its highest point was as follows in various locations: (First District) The deepest areas, Xiaopaiying and Ximen Street, were 7 feet deep. The shallowest areas, Duqueikou and Suwei Road, were 1 foot deep. The remaining areas, Xifengli, Wohuqiao, Taipingqiao, Huangdi Temple, Hupoyan, Wufuxiang, Sunlaoying, Shanhua Ward, and Jiegaoting, averaged 3 to 6 feet. (Second District) The deepest areas, Cangqian Street and Wenzao Mountain, were 9 feet deep. The shallowest areas, Tangmendou and Kuotou Street, were 1 foot deep. The remaining areas, Guanglufang, Wenrufang, Yijinfang, and Shuiliuwan, averaged 3 to 4 feet. (Third District) The deepest areas, Bangzhou, Wubao, Qishe, and Chating, were 9 feet deep. The shallowest areas, Sheren Temple and Qiaozitou, were 4 feet deep. The remaining areas, Xing'anqiao, Tanwei Street, Yangzhongting, Nanchanshanbian, and Taishan Temple, averaged 5 to 8 feet. (Fourth District) The deepest areas, Shangshu Temple and Chadao, were 7 feet deep. The shallowest area, Hechuncheng, was 2 feet deep. The remaining areas, Bailong'an, Bailongqiao, and Congpujing, averaged 4 to 6 feet. (Fifth District) The deepest areas, Longtanjiao and Lingxiayang, were 7 feet deep. The shallowest areas, Xiaduyang and Sanyijie, were 2 feet deep. The remaining areas, Fanchuanpu, Racecourse, Zhongzhou Street, Xiachi, and Taoyuan, averaged 3 to 5 feet. All bus routes were suspended for two days, the 24th and 25th, due to the excessive flooding. People used small boats to transport people or goods to and from the streets. Due to the turbulent currents, boats often capsized and people drowned. According to a survey, 5 people drowned in Taipingqiao, 3 people drowned in Chating, 2 people drowned in Jiufuan and Houtian respectively, and 1 person drowned in Nanxin Road, Panlongshe, and Sanbao respectively. Even more houses collapsed.

Page 11

Latest News Summary

The rice paddies in the southwest were being irrigated and filled, but they were washed away, resulting in extremely heavy losses. The county government, the public security bureau, and various charitable organizations cooked thin congee, guangbing cakes, and bread on the 24th and 25th and transported them to the flooded areas to provide disaster relief to the victims. Women and children in the deepest areas were rescued and housed in temples on higher ground. By the evening of the 25th, the floodwaters began to recede, but the water in the low-lying areas had not completely receded. In the areas where the water had receded, the roads were filled with piles of filth, and the stench was nauseating, which was very detrimental to hygiene. On the afternoon of the 26th, heavy rain started again, and it is feared that the floodwaters that had receded would rise again. (June 26)

Flood on the Southern Section of the Pinghan Railway 69

Traffic Between Xiping and Xuchang Temporarily Suspended

Hankou Correspondence: Due to the rising water level of the Luo River, the tracks and bridges in Mengmiaocun, Yancheng, and Guodian on the southern section of the Pinghan Railway were damaged. Since the 30th of last month, traffic between Ping and Han has not been able to pass directly. After receiving the report, Huang Zhenxing, the chairman of the Pinghan Railway Management Committee, ordered the engineering and mechanical departments to work overtime to repair the damage. The bridges and roads between Mengmiaocun and Yancheng can be repaired in three days, and the bridges and roads between Yancheng and Guodian can be repaired in four days. It may be possible to restore traffic in five days. Guan Xilin, the director of the traffic department of the committee, and Liang Yongzhang, the deputy director, telegraphed the committee on the 2nd regarding the traffic situation, stating, "Regarding the sections at 834 kilometers, which were dug up by the villagers, and 832 kilometers and 0829 meters, where the bridges were submerged by water, causing traffic disruption, we have reported this to you by telegram today. It is now reported that there has been a flash flood between Xiping and Yancheng, and the roadbed has been submerged. On the 30th of last month, the second express train from Hanbei was used as the first express train from Xiping and returned to Hankou. It is also reported that the villagers in the area between Mengmiao and Yancheng continue to dig up the roadbed to release the floodwaters. Currently, the Luo River is flooding, and the water is vast, making it difficult to predict when traffic will be restored. The first express train from Beiping on the 30th was used as the second express train from Xuzhou and returned to Beiping, etc. Therefore, except for ordering the section to temporarily use the first down express train to Xuzhou as the second express train to return, and the second up express train to Zhumadian as the first express train to return, to temporarily maintain passenger transport, we respectfully report this by telegram. Please review and approve." (July 2)

Jiangsu Provincial Party Consolidation Committee Again Submits to the Central Government to Stop the Establishment of a Prohibited-Smoking Investigation Office 70

The Jiangsu Provincial Party Consolidation Committee yesterday submitted to the central government again regarding the matter of stopping the establishment of a Prohibited-Smoking Investigation Office, stating, "We have learned from the Changshu County Executive Committee that the Ministry of Finance is establishing a National Prohibited-Smoking Office, with branch offices in each province and investigation offices in each county. We are saddened to hear this. Using prohibition as a means of taxation is enough to fuel the flames of addiction. This is a suicidal policy for the party and the nation. Unless they want to cut themselves off from the public, how can they bear to do this? We urge you again to push the central government to strictly stop this. The salt telegram is extremely urgent and awaits orders." This case was previously submitted by the committee to your council for prohibition, but no reply has been received to date. According to recent newspaper reports, more specific details have been revealed, which has caused even greater confusion across the country. Based on the telegram, we are submitting this document again for your review and approval, and we urge you to quickly stop this to curb the scourge of drugs and to meet the expectations of the people. This is truly a benevolent act. Respectfully submitted to the Central Executive Committee (3rd)

Major Scandal in the Wuhu Legal Community 71

Lawyers Association Accuses Judges of Malfeasance and Bribery

Lawyers Also Mutually Accuse Each Other of Bribery and Opium Use

Wuhu Correspondence: After the incident of the assault on Xu Shaolou, a clerk of the local court, at the Star Film Theater in Wuhu, public opinion outside was in an uproar. Rumors of collusion between judges and lawyers and blatant bribery were also rife. The Lawyers Association believed that the malfeasance and bribery of a few judges in the Wuhu court had become increasingly rampant, and it was difficult to tolerate the undesirable elements in the Lawyers Association who were harming the group. It was necessary to eradicate them. Therefore, it resolutely convened a special general meeting a few days ago and invited Deng Jingluan, the chief prosecutor of the court, to attend and supervise. Evidence was obtained for a total of three cases of accusation against judges and lawyers. (1) In the case of the assault on Xu Shaolou, a clerk of the court, at the Star Film Theater, according to the report of witness Chen Zhiqin, in addition to Xu Shaolou himself receiving 1,000 yuan, lawyers She Honghao and Li Weixin openly colluded with prosecutors Pei Xiyu and Da Shiying, committing malfeasance, extorting money, and seeking bribes, eventually leading to the withdrawal of the arrest warrants for Wang Yaohou and Yu Jiaodan, the managers of the Star Theater. (2) In the cases of opium offenders Peng Binchen and Chen, prosecutors Da and Pei openly solicited bribes, only imposing fines and allowing bail without detention. (3) According to member Liang Zuo's report, prosecutor Da Shiying solicited 300 yuan in bribes in the case of opium offender Han Lantian, and there are sufficient witnesses and video evidence. As a result of the meeting that day, although lawyers She Honghao and Li Weixin repeatedly defended themselves, the public resolution decided to expel them from the association and suspend their business. Regarding the accusations, in addition to sending a letter to the court requesting a reply, separate actions were taken immediately: (1) filing a complaint with the Anhui High Court and requesting a transfer of jurisdiction; (2) submitting a request to the Ministry of Judicial Administration to suspend prosecutors Pei Xiyu and Da Shiying of the Wuhu Local Court from their duties and hand them over for disciplinary action; and (3) submitting a request to the Control Yuan of the National Government to impeach them according to the law and investigate them for dismissal in accordance with the Regulations on the Punishment of Officials. Zhang Benyi and Huang Jing were designated to draft the respective complaints and accusations on the spot, and President Ge Fenglai was the legal representative of the Lawyers Association to make the accusation. It was like a thunderbolt from the blue, and the people were delighted. Unexpectedly, this morning at dawn, lawyer Huang Jing was arrested. The news spread and caused even more of a sensation. The reason was that the local court suddenly received a complaint from lawyer She Honghao last night (30th), accusing lawyers Zhang Benyi and Huang Jing and Huang's father of using opium. Everyone has the right to report opium use, and the court should accept it. Therefore, this morning, prosecutor Pei Xiyu led eight bailiffs to Huang's law firm to search it, but found nothing. He then took Huang to the court for verification. When they arrived at Zhang Benyi's office, Zhang had already gone to Shanghai for medical treatment the day before due to illness. Only an old opium pipe was found and taken to the court. Before this case broke out, lawyers Cui Xiangjiu and Lü Yiyuan and others had planned to mediate to avoid expansion. After this case occurred, the legal community was greatly shocked, because the case was complex and involved too many people, making it difficult to control. After the court took Huang to the court, it held a court session to interrogate him once. Huang firmly denied having an opium addiction and was willing to stay in the court for a few days to wait for verification. The plaintiff, She Honghao, had a stern attitude and was willing to share a room with Huang to monitor him. If the accusation was false, he was willing to accept the crime of false accusation. The court initially planned to send the two to the county chamber of commerce or the county government to find a house to live together, but as the plaintiff and defendant each disagreed, they changed to living in the lawyers' lounge of the court. What will happen to the case in the future will depend on the results of the verification. However, both the judicial and legal communities believe that this is an unfortunate event. (1st)

Wuhu Rice Industry Strike 72

The County Government Mediates, and Business Resumes on the 4th

Wuhu Correspondence: The Wuhu Guangchao Bang Rice and Grain Transportation Industry Association had a dispute with the rice industry over the issue of collecting rapeseed return fees, which triggered a rice industry strike. The members of the county chamber of commerce have repeatedly invited both parties to mediate, but because each side has taken extreme positions, nearly ten days have passed without a resolution. All industries have been affected, and the livelihood of workers is particularly alarming. County Magistrate Yu Yuying convened dozens of representatives from the transportation industry and the rice industry at the county chamber of commerce at 8:00 p.m. last night to discuss ways to resume business first, and the issues such as the return fee from before will be resolved later. It was finally decided at 10:00 p.m. that business would resume on the 4th. The resolutions are as follows: (1) From now on, the price of rice and miscellaneous grains will be settled on a net basis, and the settlement will be made according to the example of the money houses at 27 lines. In addition to the rice industry deducting commission according to regulations, all legitimate expenses of workers from before (tiē lì huí chóu zhèng gōng hú lì dǎ bó jī fāng kōng bāo xià bāo lì guò zhàn) will be paid by the grain transportation industry instead of the rice dealers. (2) The loading and unloading fees will be handled by the county magistrate's investigation of customs and the yamen. (3) Regarding the above resolution on net plate, three representatives from the transportation industry and the rice industry will convene all workers to negotiate and reach an agreement on the 3rd, and business will be allowed to resume on the 4th. The county government and the public security bureau will each issue announcements to inform the public. (3rd)

Lu Diping Takes Office as Garrison Commander of Nanchang Concurrently 73

Chiang Instructs Strict Observance of Discipline to Consolidate the Rear

Nanchang Correspondence: Chairman Chiang, based on various informants' reports that the acting garrison commander Tu Weifan was privately collecting 20,000 yuan in opium taxes every month, packaging and selling opium, and engaging in many illegal activities, dismissed Tu and handed him over to the military law department for custody and interrogation. He also appointed Lu Diping to serve as the garrison commander concurrently. After receiving the order, Lu held a swearing-in ceremony at the provincial government auditorium at 9:00 a.m. on the 1st of this month. General Commander Chiang and hundreds of guests from all walks of life attended. At about 10:00 a.m., the music began, and the meeting was held in accordance with the ritual. Chiang handed the seal of the garrison commander to Lu. After receiving the seal, Lu raised his hand and took the oath. After the oath, Chiang gave a speech, roughly saying that the communist bandits have been disturbing Jiangxi Province in recent years. Because the central government wanted to quell the rebellion, it could not devote its full efforts to eliminate them, resulting in the high flames and pervasive atmosphere of communism. Now that a large army is gathering to carry out a large-scale suppression, Nanchang is an important military and political center, and its importance is great. After I (Chiang referred to himself) came to Jiangxi, I believed that Nanchang should have good discipline and solid security, so that it could be extended to the counties. This time, Chairman Lu has condescended to take this position, and I believe that he will definitely comply with the central government's intentions and achieve the above objectives. Nanchang is the capital of Jiangxi, and discipline and security are deeply and greatly related to the future of bandit suppression. Therefore, everyone should abide by discipline and consolidate the rear, so that the front line can safely kill the bandits. The former acting garrison commander Tu Weifan has been dismissed and punished for collecting opium taxes. I hope that all civil and military officials and the public can be disciplined, because strict discipline can defeat the communist bandits and complete our mission. Then, Liu Zhenqun, a member of the Standing Committee of the Provincial Party Department, and Jiang Ji, a representative of the provincial government, delivered speeches. Finally, Lu gave a reply, roughly saying that Nanchang is the center of the province, and the responsibility of the garrison is very heavy. In the future, he will abide by the instructions of the commander-in-chief, consolidate security, and ensure that the bandit suppression soldiers have no worries. He will strictly observe discipline, and only with strict discipline can the communist bandits be defeated. However, to achieve strict discipline, it must start with oneself and set an example, so as not to leave a bad impression. Moreover, the task of the garrison is even greater than that of the police, and it has the power to supervise citizens and soldiers. On the one hand, it will strictly enforce discipline, and on the other hand, it should treat people peacefully. In particular, it will search for and eliminate all hidden communist bandits, so that the communist bandits have no possibility of activity, and then the task of bandit suppression can be completed. At about 11:00 a.m., the music was played, and the meeting was dismissed. The garrison department has moved into the provincial government office, and personnel in various departments have also been announced. Wang Shihe, the chief of the headquarters guard, is also the director of the inspection office concurrently. (June 1)

Perilous Situation at Zhukou on the Upper Reaches of the Yellow River 74

Optimistic Outlook for the Entire River This Year

Jinan Dispatch: According to the River Conservancy Bureau, the time for the summer floods of the Yellow River is approaching. Liuzhuang in Hebei Province, on the upper reaches, is prone to breaches, causing flooding in the Caozhou area of Shandong Province. Fortunately, the Hebei River Conservancy Bureau has taken notice this year and deployed resources to prevent breaches at Liuzhuang, hopefully avoiding any major issues. However, Zhukou, adjacent to Liuzhuang and within Shandong Province, is facing a dangerous situation due to rising water levels upstream. The upstream section chief has repeatedly telegraphed for urgent assistance. Zhang Lianjia, the director of the River Conservancy Bureau, has reported to the provincial government and requested 30,000 yuan for flood control, sending personnel to purchase hemp and other materials for emergency repairs. He plans to personally supervise the work at Zhukou in the next three days to prevent a breach. As for the overall situation of the river, thanks to the 200,000 yuan allocated by the provincial government for engineering work in the spring, with sufficient materials, the dikes on the upper, middle, and lower reaches have been repaired. Stone dams have been built at various dangerous points, unlike last year's dilapidated condition. Barring any unexpected major floods, the risk of a breach should be minimal. The River Conservancy Bureau's funding and engineering expenses totaled 480,000 yuan last year (240,000 yuan each), which was quite strained. This year, engineering expenses have increased to 300,000 yuan, which should be sufficient. (1st)

Shandong Silk Merchants Petition for Issuance of Public Bonds 75

Seeking Assistance Based on Jiangsu and Zhejiang Precedent

Jinan Dispatch: The Shandong Department of Agriculture and Mines previously forwarded a request from silk merchants to the Central Executive Yuan, asking for the issuance of 5 million yuan in silk industry bonds, following the precedent of Jiangsu and Zhejiang, to help the industry and maintain Shandong's position in the silk trade. The central government responded by requesting a survey of production volume as a basis for issuing the bonds. The Department of Agriculture and Mines promptly submitted a report stating that the province's annual production was at least 11,000 bales, and proposed a method of extracting an additional 30 yuan per bale as collateral for the bonds, which would generate 330,000 yuan annually, allowing for the collection of 2 million yuan in about six years. This proposal was based on rumors that the central government was willing to issue 2 million yuan. The central government has now sent another letter requesting a detailed survey of the number of silk reeling machines and the customs situation. The Department of Agriculture and Mines is still investigating the number of silk reeling machines but is expected to submit a reply soon. It is reported that most of Shandong's silk is exported through the Donghai, Jiaohai, and Jianghai customs, with only a small amount exported through the Tianjin customs. The Department of Agriculture and Mines has also sent a letter to the Shandong Provincial Party Headquarters, asking them to appeal to the central government on behalf of the province's silk merchants to protect the merchants and the silk industry. It has been found that this year's silk harvest in Shandong is very poor, unable to reach even the minimum annual production of 11,000 bales, and the losses suffered by silk merchants are becoming unbearable. The Department of Agriculture and Mines originally intended to request more than 5 million yuan in public bonds, but based on the current urgent situation, if the central government could issue 2 million yuan, it could temporarily alleviate the immediate crisis. (1st)

Jiangsu Province Abolishes Financial Bureaus in Eight Counties 76

Estimated Savings of Over 50,000 Yuan

Jiangsu Province's budget for the 19th year had a large deficit due to the actual expenditures exceeding the budget. The estimated budget for the 20th year has a deficit of over 7.7 million yuan. To avoid repeating the mistakes of the previous year, the Department of Finance is further reducing the expenses of various agencies. In addition to the merger of financial bureaus in 17 counties in April of the 19th year, the Department of Finance will abolish the financial bureaus in counties with fewer tax revenues and simpler affairs at the beginning of the 20th year. These counties include Baoshan, Funing, Shuyang, Lishui, Bao'ying, Chuansha, Haimen, and Lianshui. Following the same method as last year, the bureaus will be merged into the county governments and a section will be established, with a subsidy of 200 to 300 yuan. Overall, the annual expenses under the financial bureaus will be reduced by 76,020 yuan, while the annual subsidies to the financial sections in the counties will increase by approximately 24,000 yuan. After offsetting the increase and decrease, the actual reduction is 52,020 yuan, to conserve funds. This plan has been approved by the 410th meeting of the provincial government and instructions have been issued to the affected counties for compliance. (3rd)

Local Dispatches

Songjiang 77

Two Murder Cases in Two Days: Maluqiao, along the river, is a popular area for boating. The boatmen, mostly from Shaoxing, reside here. Today, Ma Liansheng and boat partners Wu Xiude and Zhang Changshun had a dispute with Wang Aosheng, a peddler selling pastries, because Ma was demanding payment of a debt. The dispute escalated into a group beating, and Wang Aosheng was severely injured. He was taken to St. Joseph's Hospital for treatment, but unfortunately, he succumbed to his injuries and died. This came to the attention of the deceased's cousin, Wang Baolin, who immediately reported to the Second Police Station to apprehend the perpetrators and seek justice. He also reported to the County Court, and Chief Prosecutor Zhu personally conducted an autopsy. The examination confirmed that the death was caused by the beating, and the death certificate was filled out. The three culprits, Ma Liansheng, Wu Xiude, and Zhang Changshun, were arrested while boating and taken back to the court for interrogation and legal proceedings. Furthermore, in Wulidang Township, five miles outside the North Gate, Chen Laoda married a woman surnamed Mou. Last year, she worked as a wet nurse in Shanghai and returned home. On the 22nd of last month, a man surnamed Jia from Jiangbei suddenly came to visit Chen's wife. The villagers in the area, finding his behavior suspicious, ganged up and beat him, causing him to flee with injuries. On the previous day, the man from Jiangbei returned to the area, pretending to ask a woman to wash clothes. The farmers, who were working in the fields at the time, saw him and became angry, rushing ashore to beat him, striking the back of his head with wooden sticks. He died on the 1st. The villagers involved in the attack fled. The township police reported the incident to the court, and Chief Prosecutor Zhu personally led officials on the 2nd to conduct an autopsy. Chen Laoda was taken back to the court and detained, pending the arrest and interrogation of the perpetrators.

Election of Standing Committee Members of the County Chamber of Commerce: The executive and supervisory committee members of the County Chamber of Commerce have been officially elected and took office on the afternoon of the 3rd. The executive committee members elected five standing committee members, who then elected a chairman from among themselves. As a result, Cai Zhongyu, Zhang Shengsan, Yang Zhimin, Shen Sinan, and Zhang Jiliang were elected as standing committee members, and Cai Zhongyu was elected as chairman.

Suzhou 78

Wujiang Water Patrol Rescues Hostages: According to reports, Tan Guobin, the captain of the Wujiang County Water Patrol, discovered bandit boats on the shores of Taihu Lake. On the 2nd, he personally led a team in disguise, hiring a civilian boat to set out. Upon arriving at Zhoujiadang, they encountered two bandit boats. The two sides exchanged fire for an hour. The bandits, unable to withstand the onslaught, swam away. One bandit, Lu A'wu, was captured on the spot, and one was killed. Two hostages, Shen Jizhang and Zhang Shenshi, were rescued. They were from Wuzhen, Zhejiang, and were kidnapped from their home by bandits on the 15th of the lunar March. Five people were kidnapped at the same time. Zhang Shenshi's husband was shot and killed by the bandits on the spot. Later, the bandits released Zhang Shenshi's brother-in-law, Qinglin, and Yu Hesheng's sister, Ai Bao, instructing them to prepare money to redeem Zhang Shenshi and the other hostage, otherwise they would be killed. In addition, Captain Tan intercepted one box cannon and one Mauser rifle, and handed them over to the county government. He also notified Zhang Shenshi's family in Wuzhen to come to Wujiang to take them home.

Conclusion of the Chen Zhaopeng Embezzlement Case: Chen Zhaopeng, the manager of the Bengbu branch of the National Central Bank, embezzled 26,000 yuan in 1929. The head office's Minister Song turned the case over to the Zhenjiang District Court, which sentenced Chen to two years in prison and a fine of 1,000 yuan. Chen appealed to the Suzhou High Court. On the 3rd, Zhao Zheng, the head of the criminal division, along with Prosecutor Zhu Wenzhuo, held a court session. Chen's lawyers, Lu Hongyi and Wang Bingjun, appeared in court to defend him. The judge announced the end of the debate and scheduled the verdict for the 10th of this month. Chen was returned to custody.

Fengxian 79

Formal Opening of the Tobacco Suppression and Investigation Office: The Fengxian Tobacco Suppression and Investigation Office, commissioned by Director-General Feng of the Shanghai Office, was officially opened yesterday (2nd) by Li Tianmin, the former Salt Affairs Battalion Commander of Songjiang, who rented a house belonging to the Zhuang family in the Luzha Lane. In terms of organization, in addition to the General Affairs, Accounting, and Goods Room sections, the existing defense corps in the Nanqiao district were temporarily reorganized into a protection and investigation team for inspection purposes. In various townships, investigation branches will be established, with a quota of 15,000 taels assigned to them for sales. The procedure stipulates that a deposit of 0.34 yuan per tael must be paid first to qualify. As for operating expenses, two jiao per unit will be added to the price of the goods for the branch office and three jiao for the branch, to support the operation.

Establishment of the Food Management Association: The Food Management Association, reorganized from the Warehouse Preservation Management Committee, was officially established yesterday and took over operations. In addition to the county magistrate serving as chairman, as stipulated, Shao Keren was appointed to the fund group, Cheng Weiyu to the warehouse group, and Gu Ren'an to the investigation group.

Wuxi 80

Distress Sale of Ding Shuangsheng Silk Store's Assets: After the Ding Shuangsheng silk store on the Dashiqiao in the city went bankrupt, depositors and creditors, such as Tai Daxuan, hired lawyer Tang Ying to request a court ruling. The court, after receiving the report, legally ruled that the assets and goods of the Ding Shuangsheng silk store, owned by Ding Hesheng and others, should be sold for cash and distributed by the court. It is reported that County Court President Yang, at 8 a.m. yesterday (3rd), specially sent a judge in charge of the case, along with a clerk, to the silk store to carefully assess the value of all assets and goods for sale. However, for the sake of prudence, the County Chamber of Commerce was requested to appoint experienced personnel to assist in the assessment.

Department of Finance Urges Payment of Business Tax: After the business tax amounts were determined for each industry in the county, the Department of Finance initially expressed dissatisfaction that the combined total for the county was less than 80,000 yuan, more than 60% lower than the annual target. Director Yang and others personally went to the province to explain the difficulties. The province provisionally agreed to a one-year trial period, but ordered all businesses to pay a quarter of their tax amount first and remit it to the province promptly. The County Chamber of Commerce was also requested to inform all businesses. However, many businesses remained hesitant and did not pay. The tax bureau has received only over 1,000 yuan in taxes. Compared to the determined tax amount of slightly less than 60,000 yuan, a quarter of the tax amount should be more than 10,000 yuan. Currently, it is only about one-tenth. Moreover, the Department of Finance is urging the payment of business tax as urgently as if lives depend on it. Director Yang feels that he cannot fulfill the province's expectations or gain the understanding of the merchants. He feels deeply troubled. Therefore, he went to the province for the second time to report the difficult situation to the Department of Finance. Yesterday, he returned to Wuxi and visited Qian Sunqing, the chairman of the Chamber of Commerce, requesting him to inform all businesses to consider the importance of tax revenue and make prompt payments for remittance to the province. At the same time, the County Chamber of Commerce issued a notice to all businesses in townships outside the city, setting a deadline for coming to the city to acknowledge and pay the business tax.

Changzhou 81

Chamber of Commerce Representatives Go to Province to Negotiate Business Tax: The issue of business tax acknowledgement and payment in Wuyi County has not been resolved because the amount acknowledged by each industry is too far from the amount set by the province. However, the business tax is inevitably to be implemented. The province is urging it urgently, and the provincial commissioner is staying in Changzhou to resolve it. The County Chamber of Commerce had no choice but to propose an all-county package of 50,000 yuan, with 30,000 yuan acknowledged and paid by each industry, and the remaining 20,000 yuan collected directly from businesses and rural areas that are not part of any industry.

Yangzhou 84

Husband and Wife Contend, Both Drown Themselves: Tang Xiaogouzi from Jiaji in the northern countryside married a widow surnamed Wang several years ago. Tang originally worked as a dyer in Zhenjiang, but he suffered from an eye disease and went blind, making life difficult. He took Wang to Zhenjiang to work as a wet nurse, but the woman became involved with someone else. Tang Xiaogou discovered this and forced Wang to return north with him, making life even more difficult. The couple suddenly quarreled the other day, wrestling with each other. When they reached the Tanggou area, they both fell into the river. People went to retrieve them, but they were already dead.

Qingjiang 85

County Magistrate Concurrently Serves as Director of Education: After the former director of the Huaiyin Education Bureau, Ding Zhaomin, was dismissed last winter, Fan Nongyan was appointed by the department, but Nongyan refused to take office. The Dawn of Industry in Jiangbei: The Shanghai Public Welfare Cotton Mill recently sent personnel to Pu to inspect the old copper coin buildings and incidentally investigate everything else. It is understood that the old buildings have been in disrepair for a long time and many are not suitable for use. A large number of workers will be hired to repair them soon.

Jiangyin 86

Meeting to Reorganize Local Finances: Jiangyin's local finances are in difficulty. The local agencies organized a committee to reorganize finance. On the 1st, a meeting was held at the county government, where County Magistrate Peng presented the matter for discussion, on how to formulate a plan to resolve the accumulated debt. The results of the discussion were: (1) To reorganize the busy grain collection. The finance bureau, together with the collection director, will prepare a detailed record of the accumulated debt over the years, broken down into construction, education, etc., and of the amount owed by each collection official, for verification. (2) To strictly order the collection officials to collect the old debts from the 16th, 17th, and 18th years, and to collect 20,000 yuan within two months. If any of the collection personnel resigns or attempts to evade responsibility, they will not be allowed to leave their post until they have paid off the old debts they were responsible for. (3) To issue local treasury bonds in the amount of 200,000 yuan, with a net receipt of 98%. The fund will be fixed at 0.1 yuan per mu of grain and reeds, and a committee will be organized to manage it. The interest rate will be temporarily set at 8%, and the principal and interest will be amortized monthly. A detailed charter for the issuance of treasury bonds will be drafted by the county government's finance bureau, in conjunction with the Chamber of Commerce's Property Division and the Money Trade Association. The finance bureau will be responsible for convening the local meeting. To request a provincial subsidy of 40,000 yuan, limited to one time. (4) The local funds recently collected by the finance bureau will only be handed over to the Property Division for distribution to various agencies to maintain the status quo. The debt will be discussed by the county government and the finance bureau with the creditors to defer payment.

Rugao 87

River Tide Breaches Zhengtan Sluice Gate: The No. 1 Dike in Binjiang Township, Zhengtan District, which borders the Yangtze River, has a sluice gate on its southwest end that has been in disrepair for many years. On the 19th of this month, the river tide suddenly rose sharply and breached the sluice gate. Fortunately, the farmers temporarily set up a lattice bank, and the fields were not flooded. It is said that this sluice gate is related to the annual income of the dike and the repair costs are high. The people of the dike have presented another petition to the county government, requesting that the remaining funds from the dike construction be allocated to subsidize the start of the work.

Cai Caiming's Body Covered in Wounds: Cai Caiming, of Dayu Town, Juegang, was murdered. The Jiangsu High Court specially sent Zhou Baochu, a judge from the Zhenjiang District Court, to Rugao to conduct a coffin inspection. It is understood that Zhou, accompanied by Tang, the trial judge, and Guo Yongming, the clerk and inspector, went to the Tea Temple outside the West Gate at 8 a.m. yesterday to open the coffin for inspection. After Guo, the inspector, boiled the bones according to law, it was found that there were slight red wounds on the nostrils, teeth, skull, and foot bones. It is said that he died by hanging himself after being injured. After the inspection, the bones were collected. Judge Zhou and others returned to the province yesterday afternoon to report.

Gaoyou 88

Bandit Raids on Cargo Ship in Luyang Lake: A small number of bandits have recently been discovered in Luyang Lake, which connects Gaoyou and Yangzhou. At around 5 p.m. on the afternoon of the previous day, a cargo ship sailing from Yangzhou to Fanchuan encountered several bandits who ordered it to stop and swarmed aboard, searching extensively. It is reported that silver dollars and goods were looted, resulting in significant losses.

Bandits Rob Qiushuge Pavilion: At around 7 p.m. on the afternoon of the previous day, several bandit ships suddenly arrived from Luyang Lake at Qiushuge Pavilion, which connects Gaoyou and Yangzhou. More than a dozen bandits, each armed with guns, speaking with a Yancheng accent, moored and landed to search and loot separately. After four hours, they fired their guns and left. It is estimated that more than twenty households were robbed, resulting in significant losses.

Unable to Pay Grain Tax, Intends to Commit Suicide: Wu Shixing, a farmer from Zhetuo Town in the Sixth District of the county, comes from a well-off family with hundreds of acres of farmland. However, in recent years, he has suffered from repeated droughts and is heavily in debt. In addition, he has been urged by the grain tax collectors to pay the grain tax, leaving him desperate. He conceived the idea of ending his life and purchased more than a dozen firecrackers, intending to swallow them. Fortunately, his wife saw him and snatched them away.

[P Nanjing

Central Industrial Experiment Institute Enrolls Students for Training: The Central Industrial Experiment Institute of the Ministry of Industry has been in operation for one year and has achieved remarkable results. In order to cultivate skilled industrial personnel, the Institute has specially established a crafts training school this year to recruit new students, teaching them industrial knowledge and emphasizing practical factory training to gain practical manufacturing experience. The Institute's mechanical workshop has already enrolled students once. Now the chemical workshop is also recruiting new students. It is heard that there has been a large number of applicants recently.

Jiaxing 89

Reasons for the Resignation of the Third District Chief: Pan Qinghua, the chief of the Wangjiangjing Third District of Jiaxing, has always been very impetuous in his work and suffers from many hidden illnesses. Therefore, there has been a lot of complaints from outsiders. This time, he also heard that the Wancheng Rice Store in the town was searched, which led to a strike in the rice industry. Pan felt that it would be increasingly difficult to handle matters in the future, so he decided to resign to the Department of Civil Affairs.

Opening of the Vagrant Vocational Training Center: The Jiaxing Vagrant Vocational Training Center has been actively prepared and was opened the other day. The county Clearing and Strengthening Bureau specially transferred 24 vagrants who had been arrested (three were suspected of being bandits, three were notorious local bullies, and 18 were genuine vagrants) to the county government and sent them to the Vagrant Vocational Training Center for acceptance.

Hangzhou 90

Payment of Arrears by Two County Magistrates: The arrears owed by former magistrates and county chiefs of various counties in Zhejiang Province amounted to a huge sum of 1.3 to 1.4 million. The Department of Finance of the provincial government has published a list in the newspaper, ordering them to pay in full within one month. If they delay further, they will be reported and arrested. It is heard that Xu Zhilong, the former magistrate of Xianju County, has presented most of his arrears of 2,758 yuan in cash, and the remaining arrears can also be guaranteed to be paid on time. Zong Shinian, the former magistrate of Haining County, has also paid his arrears in full.

More Mutineers Escorted to Province: Soldiers of the 16th Company of the 7th Regiment of the Zhejiang Provincial Security Corps recently mutinied in their garrison in Xincang, Pinghu. Regiment Commander Shen Guocheng led troops to pursue and capture more than 30 mutineers, including a platoon leader, and they have been escorted to Hangzhou for detention. It is learned that Cao Pang, the temporary commander for bandit suppression in Jingsongjiaping, has captured two more mutineers, Zhang Shiyong and Fang Fengtian, in Zhangyan Town. After questioning them, he instructed the Security Office to send officials to escort them. They were escorted to the province yesterday. The provincial government has ordered them to be detained and interrogated.

Township Museum Director Suddenly Suspended by County Government: Xu Deyang, the director of the Zhenhai County Township Public Education Museum, has been in office for four months since his appointment, and has achieved remarkable results. Anhui 92

Foreign Warehouses Outside Xiangkou Ordered to Move Quickly: In order to avoid inspection, the foreign warehouses of Wanhuayang, Riqing, and Jardine companies have been privately moved to Xiangkou, across from Wanhuayang. Xuanwuguang Automobile Road to be Taken Over by the Government: The automobile road from Wuhu to Xuancheng and Guangde was originally run by merchants. The roadbed is borrowed from the unfinished Ningxiang Road. Due to insufficient funds, there has been little development. The company has submitted a request to the Construction Department to take it over and run it by the government. The Construction Department is currently sending personnel to investigate.

Local News

Shanghai Municipal Boy Scout Council Holds Service Personnel Registration 97

Deadline: One Month

The Shanghai Municipal Boy Scout Council of China issued a notice yesterday to conduct a preliminary registration of all Boy Scout service personnel in the city. The notice stated: “It has recently been discovered that among the service personnel in the city, many have not completed the procedures for reporting departures or arrivals, and have either left the city without permission or gone to serve in various countries directly. This kind of action is highly inconvenient for the progress of the Council’s work. Therefore, the 16th standing committee of the Council has resolved to hold a city-wide registration of service personnel again from July 1st to 31st. All Chinese Boy Scout service personnel who are still working or residing in the city next semester must complete the relevant procedures within the specified dates. In addition to enclosing a copy of the 20th-year re-registration form for Shanghai Municipal Boy Scout service personnel, this notice is hereby issued for compliance.”

Lao University Students' Declaration to Continue Enrollment (Continued) 99

The school and the students are like a country and its citizens. A country cannot be a country without citizens, and similarly, how can a school be a school without students? Our university once suspended enrollment, and now all the first-term students are graduating this year. Looking at the entire university department, only four classes remain in the three colleges of engineering, agriculture, and social sciences, with just over a hundred students. If enrollment continues to be suspended, how can this be a university? This is the first reason why enrollment cannot be suspended again this year. Currently, China's rural economy is facing a total crisis. Farmers' children cannot afford huge education expenses, and are generally prevented by money from attending school. The revolutionary youths who are out of school can no longer bear to see this. Our university is responsible for cultivating leading talents to implement the Three People's Principles of agriculture and industry, and has established a free education policy. The general poor youth are looking forward to the early enrollment of our university. Therefore, for the sake of expanding the training of revolutionary talents and relieving the poor revolutionary youths who are out of school, this is the second reason why enrollment cannot be suspended again this year. Since our university is a product of a certain era and society, and has the mission of seeking the liberation of the working masses of farmers and workers, then at a time when the national revolutionary atmosphere is low and the farmers, workers, and students are disheartened, it is necessary to actively train leading talents for the farmers' and workers' movement in order to achieve the thorough success of the revolution. Now, repeatedly suspending enrollment is tantamount to expelling revolutionary youths and violating the Three People's Principles of agriculture and industry. Therefore, for the sake of the future development of the revolution, this is the third reason why enrollment cannot be suspended again this year. Furthermore, reorganizing the school and enrolling students do not conflict at all. The so-called reorganization is just to get rid of the old and bring in the new in the school's affairs, and it is by no means to not want students. If there are no students, how can we talk about reorganization? Only enrollment is a practical reorganization. Otherwise, there is only the name of reorganization, but no one knows how to reorganize or how to reorganize. We reorganized last year, reorganized this year, and will reorganize again next year. The future of Lao University is over. Therefore, for the sake of promoting the future of labor education and developing the future of Lao University, this is the fourth reason why enrollment cannot be suspended again this year. In conclusion, at a time when the revolutionary tide is high around the world and the working masses of farmers and workers are in urgent need of liberation, labor education has become a certain educational trend ahead of the times, and the Lao University is in particular urgent need in China. Therefore, enrollment is the life-or-death point of our university. It is necessary in objective fact, and it should also be in subjective principle. We deeply believe that the Ministry of Education must have the determination to develop labor education and the enthusiasm to maintain our university, and will not destroy the existence of our university or have the selfish intention of destroying labor education, and will not bear to make the poor revolutionary youths across the country fall into a state of being out of school, causing the future of the national farmers' and workers' movement to become dim. All the students of the University Department of our university have seen this, so we dare to show our sincerity and respectfully ask the people of the society to understand and help, and even hope that the Ministry of Education will take into account the current facts and adhere to the original intention of loving labor education, and immediately withdraw the order to suspend the enrollment of our university, then our university will be fortunate, the future of labor education will be fortunate, and the poor youth who are out of school across the country will be fortunate! (End)

Local News

Shanghai-Fujian Vessels to Be Searched Starting Today 113

To Prevent Red Bandits from Mixing into Fujian Province

After the Jiangxi Communists were attacked by the central armies, they are now under a general siege. Commander-in-Chief Chiang Kai-shek telegraphed the Fujian Provincial Government and the naval authorities, stating that the communist army will launch a large-scale attack soon, and that there is concern that the Red Bandits will flee to the Fujian border. He ordered that strict precautions be taken. The provincial government and the naval authorities agreed to strictly prevent the Red Bandits from mixing into Fujian and implemented inspections. The inspection office organized by the Provincial Maritime Association has notified all Chinese and foreign shipping companies in this city that starting today, all ships traveling from Shanghai to Fujian, the entry of passengers, and their luggage must be strictly inspected. Those whose behavior is suspicious will be immediately detained. In order to avoid delaying the voyage of the ships, the shipping companies have agreed with the inspection office that when Shanghai ships arrive in Minjiang, members of the inspection office will board the ships at the mouth of Minjiang to carry out searches, so that the searches can be completed on board when the ships arrive at Mawei, so as to avoid inspections after arriving at the port, causing various obstacles and disputes. The Fujian authorities have already agreed to this method. Shanghai-Fuzhou ships will be inspected starting today.

Reasons for Stagnation in Shanghai-Fujian Shipping 114

Fuzhou Flood Disaster

Since the arrival of Fuzhou liners in Fujian, there have been frequent delays and cancellations. The Sannong Company's Wanxiang ship arrived in Shanghai yesterday from Fuzhou. To understand the reasons for the shipping obstruction, the reporter specifically visited shipowner Mr. Liu to inquire about everything. Only then did they learn of the unprecedented tragedy of the great flood disaster in Fuzhou. Fields and homes were completely submerged, and corpses were exposed. This has also caused significant losses to Shanghai-Fujian shipping. Details are recorded as follows:

Nantai Turns into a Marshland Fuzhou's great flood disaster began on June 26th. Continuous heavy rain caused mountain torrents to erupt. The water source flowed from Yanping into the Min River and rushed towards Nantai. Nantai is the most prosperous commercial area in Fuzhou, with many large shops. The sudden flood turned all the streets of Nantai into marshlands. At the height of the flood, the water level was about one zhang [~3 meters], and all the shops and residences were submerged. People escaping from the streets had to navigate in boats. Goods were washed away, houses collapsed, and people were displaced. The magnitude of the loss and the severity of the disaster have been rare in recent years.

Corpses Block the River The Sannong Wanxiang ship, traveling from Shanghai to Fujian, was entering the Min River and arriving at Mawei on the second day of the great flood disaster. Along the way, they saw corpses floating in the Min River, drifting downstream. No one was retrieving and burying them. These corpses were mostly from Nantai and the outside of Fuzhou city who had drowned. They were washed downstream. Along the river, there were also broken goods and materials from collapsed houses. The sight was everywhere.

Customs House Immersed in Water The Min Customs House is located in Haiguan Cheng [Customs Square], which was also flooded. This caused the Customs House buildings to be submerged in water. The lower-level offices had become rivers. Staff members had to move to the top floor. Customs officials and merchants reporting and paying taxes had to arrive by boat. However, due to the flood, the work of the Customs House was almost completely stopped.

Shipping Stopped by the Flood Fuzhou's export goods were usually transported by barge from the city to the pier for loading onto ships. Since the flood disaster occurred, many goods have been washed away or damaged by the water. Those that were not affected by the water were unable to be transported because the Min River was flooded, and barges could not carry cargo. As a result, shipping was suspended for three days, delaying all Shanghai-bound merchant ships. The Wanxiang ship was delayed by more than three days and nights, and other merchant ships were delayed by four or five days. Loading only began at the end of June. However, the incoming cargo had been greatly reduced, and merchants had stopped transporting goods. As a result, the Wanxiang arrived in Shanghai with only 20-30% of its capacity. Mr. Liu also said that when the ship left Fujian, the water had not completely receded. Shanghai's shipments to Fujian would also be severely affected.

Chen Shaokuan Returns to Shanghai Due to Illness 115

Did Not Land at Xiangshan

Chen Shaokuan, Navy Deputy Minister and Director of the Jiangnan Shipyard, took the Xin Ning Shao ship to Ningbo at 5 p.m. one day. After arriving in Ningbo on the morning of the 2nd, he transferred to the Yixian warship waiting in Ningbo to go to Xiangshan. At 10 a.m. that morning, after the ship left Ningbo, Mr. Chen suddenly felt unwell, with severe abdominal pain. It was probably due to heatstroke. Therefore, Mr. Chen passed by Xiangshan, only met with Zeng Yiding, commander of the torpedo fleet, and did not go ashore to inspect the naval school. Moreover, the ship lacked medical care, so Mr. Chen stayed there for a short time and then ordered the ship to return to Shanghai. Mr. Chen arrived in Shanghai yesterday (the 3rd) morning at 7 a.m. on the Yixian warship and immediately summoned naval hospital medical officers for diagnosis. He is currently staying at the Astor House Hotel on the Bund.

The Wusong Songyang Telephone Company has been in operation for eight years. International Wireless Telegraph Price Reduction 118

Implemented from the 10th of this Month

Saigon Communication Realized on the 1st

Reducing Telegraph Fees The International Telecommunications Bureau believes that the price of gold has recently fallen slightly, and the established international wireless telegraph prices should be reduced to benefit business. Therefore, it has formulated new telegraph fees, which will be implemented from the 10th of this month. It is reported that the new price is one-tenth lower than the old price.

Saigon Communication All wireless telegraphs between Shanghai and Saigon have been unilaterally received and sent by the French radio station in Gujiazhai, which exceeded its authority. Now that the French radio station has stopped receiving and sending commercial telegrams, the French side has requested that the bureau communicate directly with Saigon. This has been realized since the 1st. However, this is limited to Shanghai. The rates for other places such as Xiamen are still under discussion. Once resolved, communication with Saigon can also be implemented.

Night Telegraphs Night telegraphs to the United States, the Philippines, and other places have previously been limited to a minimum of 20 words per message. It has now been decided to change this to a minimum of 25 words per message, which will be implemented in the coming days.

Installing Telephones in the Area of Roads Built Beyond the Boundary 119

Talks by Huang Boqiao, Director of the Municipal Bureau of Public Utilities

The issue of installing telephones in the area of roads built beyond the boundary has not been resolved, and there are doubts from the outside world. Reporters from various newspapers believe that telephone communications are important, so they went to the responsible Municipal Bureau of Public Utilities to investigate the truth. According to Director Huang, the city's telephone service is handled by the Shanghai Telephone Bureau of the Ministry of Communications. The telephone company in the concession installed telephones in the area of roads built beyond the boundary based on an attachment to the communication contract signed between the Shanghai Telephone Bureau of the Ministry of Communications and the former Shanghai China-Foreign Telephone Company. This contract was signed on December 17th, 1925, for a period of five years, expiring on December 16th, 1930. After the Shanghai Telephone Company acquired the former China-Foreign Telephone Company, it did not express any opinion on the expiring contract. Now that the contract has long expired, the company has no basis for installing telephones in the area of roads built beyond the boundary. The Public Utilities Bureau believes that the area of roads built beyond the boundary belongs to the Chinese area, and the company should not operate beyond the boundary. Now that the basis has been lost, the company naturally cannot install any more telephones in the area of roads built beyond the boundary. Even the existing telephone sets and poles should be completely removed. However, the residents in this area have a great need for telephones. Before the Shanghai Telephone Bureau of the Ministry of Communications can reach this area, it cannot be taken care of. Under appropriate conditions, another good solution will be discussed. Although the city's telephone service is operated by the Ministry of Communications, the municipal government, for the convenience of the citizens, should do its best to assist. Therefore, on the day after the expiration of the aforementioned communication contract, December 17th, 1930, it immediately invited the Director of the Shanghai Telephone Bureau of the Ministry of Communications and the General Manager of the Shanghai Telephone Company to discuss and orally suggested establishing a temporary contract so that the citizens who already had telephones would not be interrupted and those who did not have them could install them. Afterwards, after several meetings, in order to quickly resolve the issue, it drafted a draft contract on May 22nd, inviting representatives from both parties to the bureau to discuss it. The representative of the Shanghai Telephone Company stated that there were still aspects of the contract conditions that needed to be studied and requested that the draft contract be taken back for study and that opinions be submitted as soon as possible to schedule another meeting for final decision. Only because the Shanghai Telephone Company had not expressed its opinion for a long time had this issue been delayed. The Public Utilities Bureau repeatedly requested the Shanghai Telephone Bureau of the Ministry of Communications to urge the company to express its views as soon as possible and practically. Finally, on June 26th and 27th, the Director of the Telephone Bureau and the General Manager of the company came to the bureau to continue the discussion. As a result, all the conditions in the contract were discussed, and only the wording needed to be refined before it could be formally signed. The issue of installing telephones in the area of roads built beyond the boundary will be resolved in the near future.

Holding Grand Celebrations

Today is the 155th anniversary of the United States' declaration of independence. American communities around the world are holding grand celebrations. However, because the US Consulate General building is being renovated, it is temporarily renting the former Kaili Hotel site on Jiangxi Road, which is relatively narrow. Therefore, invitations were not sent out as widely as in previous years. The American business community will also participate in the parade. The flag-raising ceremony will be held at the Racecourse immediately after the review ceremony. Because of the parade, speeches and the reading of the Declaration of Independence will be omitted. At noon, US Consul General Cunningham will receive congratulations and entertain guests at the consulate. In the afternoon, the amateur baseball association and the US Marine Corps (i.e., the McLain team) will play a baseball game at the Racecourse. The American Club will also hold a grand celebratory banquet. The Public Concession Police Station, fearing that the parade at the Racecourse and the congratulations at the US Consulate General would cause traffic congestion, has designated parking locations and stipulated that after the parade is over, vehicles traveling west on Nanjing Road must detour via Xizang Road. Record of the Silk Factory Trade Association Meeting 124

Many Objections to the Allocation of Public Bonds

Wage Issue to be Mediated Next Week

The Shanghai Silk Factory Trade Association held its tenth plenary meeting of the trade association yesterday (the 3rd) at 4 p.m. Over 100 representatives of silk factories attended, including Zhu Jing'an, Wu Shenbo, and Sun Rongchang. Chairman Shen Huachen presided over the meeting. The chairman first reported that the Shanghai Municipality is implementing unified weights and measures, and the Social Bureau has been sending personnel to factories and businesses since July 1st to conduct strict inspections. Violators will be punished. Although the foreign silk market uses pounds for the UK and the US and meters for France, the scales used by the factories must be replaced immediately. Those who rent factories should immediately notify the landlord. Those who own their own factories should immediately go to the Social Bureau to apply for new-style scales to ensure uniformity and avoid punishment. Next, he reported on the issue of female workers' wages. Representatives of labor and management were convened twice for mediation. The trade association intended to comply with the Wuxi method of increasing wages to 57 cents, but the workers were not understanding and held different opinions. A mediation meeting must be held next week to resolve the issue. Then, it was discussed that the Ministry of Industry ordered that double-cocoon silk factories not be allowed to enjoy the distribution of silk industry public bonds, and the customs for the export of double-cocoon silk has also stopped collecting special taxes. However, there are only six double-cocoon silk factories in Shanghai, all of which are members of the association, and it is actually difficult for them to make a profit. They should be treated the same as those receiving relief. It was decided that the reasons would be stated at the fifth executive committee meeting of the Silk Industry Public Bond Special Committee today (the 4th) to request the allocation of bond certificates. Next, the issue of the issuance of silk industry public bonds was discussed. Chairman Shen stated that the Ministry of Finance bond certificates could be printed by July 10th and could be issued by the deadline. All members of the trade association should list the amount of silk in stock and the number of machines within three days and register with the association for allocation. The seals of the factory director and the person receiving the bond certificates should also be sent to the association for compilation and reporting to the ministry for the issuance of repayment certificates. Do not delay. As for the 2 million yuan for improved machinery and boiling cocoon machines, bond certificates of 3,000 yuan will be issued for each machine and 2,000 yuan for each black board machine. However, the price of this machinery is quite high, and only 2,000-3,000 yuan is issued per machine, plus the discount on public bonds, it is difficult to cover the cost. If the bond amount of 2 million yuan for the improved machinery is given to the landlord, the same industry members will have worked hard to obtain the issuance of public bonds, while the landlord will sit back and enjoy the benefits, which is difficult for them to accept. At this point, the atmosphere at the meeting became tense, and the representatives opposed it. Later, it was decided that the situation in Shanghai would be presented to the Special Committee for further deliberation. Next, the case of the silkworm seed crackdown was discussed. The representatives present all expressed their opposition to supporting this institution, which is detrimental to the same industry, with public bonds. Finally, the representatives discussed with each other and then adjourned the meeting, which was already past 7 p.m.
