The National Government Will Reject the Sichuan Public Bonds 128

Yesterday a letter was sent to the Sichuan Native Place Association

The Sichuan Native Place Association in Shanghai had previously requested the National Government to reject Liu Xiang and Liu Wenhui's issuance of post-war public bonds and provincial public bonds. Yesterday, the Secretariat of the National Government sent a letter to the association, which began by stating that they received a document from the Chief Secretary, forwarded by the Chairman, requesting the rejection of Liu Xiang and Liu Wenhui's issuance of public bonds under false pretenses, in order to eliminate the source of chaos and alleviate the people's suffering. The directive stated that the matter had been forwarded to the Executive Yuan, and that a letter had been sent to inform them accordingly. At the same time, the association is still paying close attention to this matter. In addition to submitting a petition to the Legislative Yuan to prevent the passage of the two Liu's public bond regulations and sending letters to Dai Jitao and the Sichuan Native Place Association in Beijing to jointly oppose them, they also plan to send representatives to Beijing to petition the national government. The express telegram from the association is recorded below:

To all national agencies, organizations, and newspapers, to all Sichuan agencies, organizations, newspapers, and elders, to all Sichuan native place associations across the country for forwarding to all compatriots abroad, and to all Shanghai-based Sichuan organizations for forwarding to all compatriots in Shanghai: The following is a copy of a petition recently submitted by our association to the National Government: "Petition requesting the rejection of Liu Xiang and Liu Wenhui's issuance of public bonds under false pretenses, in order to eliminate the source of chaos in Sichuan and alleviate the people's suffering." According to letters from mass organizations in Chengdu, Chongqing, and other places in Sichuan, Liu Xiang, the Director-General of Post-War Affairs in Sichuan, and Liu Wenhui, the Chairman of the Sichuan Provincial Government, plan to request the Central Government's approval to issue public bonds to fund the civil war. They instructed our association to prevent this from happening in the vicinity. We were surprised and at the same time, we saw reports in newspapers in Beijing and Shanghai stating that Liu Xiang's representatives had requested the issuance of 20 million yuan in Sichuan small post-war public bonds, and the government had forwarded it to the Legislative Yuan for deliberation. At the same time, Liu Wenhui also requested to follow Liu Xiang's example and issue 20 million yuan in Sichuan provincial public bonds, and the government is also reviewing it. Our association believes that this matter is of great concern to the interests of the people of Sichuan, and it is difficult to remain silent and endure it. Furthermore, since the Central Government has repeatedly declared that it seeks public opinion, we must express our views frankly. Therefore, we respectfully present to your government the absurdity of the two Liu's request to issue public bonds. Sichuan Province has been in a state of chaos in recent years, with over 300,000 troops rampaging and engaged in internal strife. The grain taxes in various places have been pre-collected until the 34th year of the Republic (1945), and each county has one or two dozen types of miscellaneous taxes, with a total of 120 million yuan being extorted each year. Although the Central Government has clearly ordered the abolition of likin and the elimination of excessive taxes, the various military bandits have turned a blind eye and even intensified their efforts. Our poor people rely entirely on traditional agricultural production for their livelihoods, and there is no large-scale industrial and commercial economy to regulate it. They are taking flesh to heal sores and scraping skin to the bone. The people's strength is exhausted, and how can they bear it? In addition, in the past two years, disasters have struck simultaneously. The mountains and rivers of Sichuan are filled with wailing. In the prosperous towns of Sichuan, over 100 well-known businesses have closed down. Rice and grain are in short supply everywhere, and begging for food and transportation has spread throughout the Yangtze River area. Refugee unrest is rampant in various counties, and various forms of disturbances are being carried out by religious bandits and communists. This situation cannot reach the ears of the emperor due to the barrier of the Kui Gate. However, Commissioners Ding Chao-wu and Fang Jue-hui have personally visited the area and can easily prove everything. If, in the midst of this dying population, they are suddenly forced to pay 40 million yuan in public bonds, and there are no wealthy merchants to provide assistance, it will not only leave the majority of disaster victims without any means of survival, but if it creates a red disaster like Jiangxi, who will bear the responsibility? Therefore, we request that your government take into account the suffering of the people and reject it. This is the first reason. The Sichuan region is currently divided among various military forces. In addition to the two Liu's, Deng Xihou, Tian Songyao, Yang Sen, and Liu Cunhou also occupy their own territories and do not yield to each other. Although the two Liu's are in charge of military and political affairs, they only have a Post-War Affairs Directorate and a provincial government. If they truly supported the Central Government and sought to unify Sichuan, our people would be willing to endure and bear these public bonds. However, neither of the two Liu's wants to unify Sichuan. They are preoccupied with seeking the development of their personal power and obtaining more counties and defense areas or more divisions and troops, which is enough to satisfy their desires. The most obvious example is the recent war in northern Sichuan. Li Jiayu was recruited by Liu Xiang, but Liu Wenhui attacked him. Chen Guangzao was recruited by Liu Wenhui, but Liu Xiang attacked him. The two Liu's are clearly taking opposing actions, but in reality, the two are not enemies. Recently, they even met in Chongqing, claiming to be senior officials appointed by the Central Government and jointly seeking to unify Sichuan. They do not hesitate to sacrifice the lives and property of millions of people to provide them with a performance of farcical, contradictory, and confusing internal warfare, which is truly ridiculous. Now they want to issue public bonds under false pretenses to continue expanding their unspeakable internal warfare. In addition to benefiting them personally, the harm to the country and the people is almost indescribable. If your government does not examine the use of the public bonds and approves their issuance, it will be tantamount to fueling the internal chaos in Sichuan, destroying the government's credibility, and placing the 70 million people of Sichuan in a death trap. Therefore, we request that your government take into account the elimination of the chaos in Sichuan and reject it. This is the second reason. The two Liu's occupy the most defense areas in Sichuan. Liu Xiang occupies more than 40 counties, and Liu Wenhui occupies more than 60 counties. The fertile land in southeastern Sichuan is entirely owned by them. Everyone knows the wealth they have accumulated through years of extortion. In addition to opening banks and shops in Chengdu and Chongqing and acquiring vast fields in western Sichuan to build a rich and prosperous foundation for their descendants for generations to come, they are also making every effort to expand their military equipment, establishing arsenals throughout the province and purchasing new weapons from abroad to use as tools to suppress the people. The people of Sichuan are suffering greatly from too many soldiers. The only way to save the people of Sichuan is through demobilization. However, the two Liu's not only do not demobilize a single soldier but continue to increase their numbers. What is the purpose of this? Is it as Chairman Chiang said, that there is no need for demobilization, and that they will be used to undertake national defense and pacify the local areas? However, western Kang has already been conquered, but we have not heard of Liu Wenhui increasing his troops to go to Kang. Western Hubei is on the verge of becoming a bandit area, but we have not seen Liu Xiang sending more troops out of Sichuan. Now, with insatiable greed, they are not satisfied with extorting the people to enrich themselves and hoarding troops for self-defense, and they are still asking the Central Government to explicitly approve the issuance of public bonds to fill their insatiable desires. Their inhumanity has reached this point. Even if they take all the property of the people of Sichuan and offer it to these people, they may still ask the Central Government to bear their military and political expenses. Therefore, we request that your government take into account the punishment of corruption and reject it. This is the third reason. Even if we take a step back and say that the two Liu's public bonds are truly used to handle post-war affairs in Sichuan, we should bear it. However, their claim to use Sichuan's stamp tax and tobacco and alcohol tax to offset the public bond fund is also unreliable. What is the reason? When Sichuan's soldiers raise funds from the people, they are mostly called loans or advances, but the result is always that there is borrowing without repayment and advances without recovery. The facts are all there and can be checked one by one. This time, it is said that stamp, tobacco, and alcohol taxes will be used as collateral, but in fact, the monthly income from all stamp, tobacco, and alcohol taxes in the two Liu's defense areas is only a few hundred thousand yuan. They have claimed to use it as collateral for borrowing from the people countless times. However, although they claim to use it as collateral, they still do not repay the people, and the situation remains the same. Even if they truly respect the Central Government's prestige this time and actually allocate the funds for repayment, it should be known that although this public bond is called a post-war public bond, it is actually Liu Xiang's public bond. Although the provincial public bond is called a provincial public bond, it is actually Liu Wenhui's public bond. In recent years, the troops in Sichuan have been rising and falling, and the defense areas have been changing, with no fixed situation. Once the two Liu's move or fail, their so-called allocation will be completely ineffective. Even if the Central Government has an order to recognize it, what can it do if the local soldiers do not comply? Therefore, we request that your government take into account the maintenance of the public bond's credit and reject it. This is the fourth reason. Sichuan is a province. The so-called post-war affairs should be planned for the overall situation. However, Liu Xiang requested the issuance of a post-war public bond, and Liu Wenhui followed suit and requested the issuance of a provincial public bond. This is tantamount to treating Sichuan as two regions. How can there be any unified thought to speak of? Now, one province is issuing two types of public bonds. If other provinces also use false pretenses and follow suit, I am afraid that all kinds of public bonds will spread throughout the country. The people's strength is limited. How can they bear it? For the time being, we will not discuss whether the Central Government will allow the provinces to follow suit. However, the soldiers in Sichuan other than the two Liu's will definitely follow suit. There is no doubt about it. It is true that Deng Xihou, Tian Songyao, Yang Sen, Liu Cunhou, etc., do not have legitimate reasons to ask the Central Government to issue public bonds. However, as long as the Central Government approves the issuance by the two Liu's, they can freely do so. We do not know how many more public bonds will appear in Sichuan Province. According to Sichuan's military convention, if Army A draws a certain type of tax, Army B and Army C will certainly draw a certain type of tax, regardless of whether Army A has submitted it to the Central Government for approval. For example, in the past, when Liu Xiang submitted a request to the Central Government to handle special taxes, the various armies also handled special taxes themselves, and the people did not dare to resist. The reason they held was that Army A was raising funds for military expenses, and our army could also raise funds for military expenses. If the people dared to oppose it, they would be accused of resisting the public and being enemies of the people, and they would suffer unforeseen disasters. Therefore, we request that your government take into account the elimination of the abuse of public bonds and reject it. This is the fifth reason. Based on the above five points, in order to protect the glorious history of our party and the National Revolutionary Army, we do not want the troops of Sichuan to stain the pure jade of the National Revolution. In order to respect our homeland and prevent the elders from perishing, we are expressing our views with hair disheveled and hat askew, shedding tears of blood. It is only appropriate to submit our respectful words and earnestly request that your government treat the people as if they were injured, not neglecting those in distant places, and approve the rejection of Liu Xiang and Liu Wenhui's request to issue post-war public bonds and provincial public bonds, so that the people of Sichuan can have a way out of the boiling pot and a ray of dawn in the dark world. We offer our most sincere prayers. Sincerely submitted. On the same day, we also sent a telegram to Liu Fucheng, Director-General Liu, and Liu Wenhui, Chairman Liu, which read: "Urgent to Director-General Liu Fucheng in Chongqing and Chairman Liu Zigan: We have repeatedly read reports stating that Director-General Fucheng has requested the Central Government to approve the issuance of 20 million yuan in Sichuan post-war public bonds, which the Central Government has not yet approved. Chairman Zigan has also followed suit and requested the issuance of 20 million yuan in provincial public bonds, which is shocking. At the same time, our association has also received letters from mass organizations in Chengdu and Chongqing and compatriots in Shanghai, requesting our association to forward them to the Central Government to stop it. Our association believes that in recent years, Sichuan Province has been plagued by disasters, and commerce has been in decline, which you are well aware of. If you are truly committed to the revolution, you should find ways to demobilize the troops and appease the survivors in order to save our people from fire and water. However, the Central Government has entrusted you with the important task of saving Sichuan, and we have never heard of any proper ways to unify Sichuan and alleviate the people's suffering. As far as our colleagues know, you are only expanding your personal military power and creating unnecessary internal strife to satisfy your personal desires, even at the expense of prolonging likin and miscellaneous taxes and increasing the local burden to further afflict our people. Our association has received repeated reports from our hometown, urging us to find ways to raise funds, with every word filled with tears, which is unbearable to read. However, considering that the various armies in Sichuan are all birds of a feather, before the Central Government can resolve the situation in Sichuan, even if we cry bitterly in the Qin court, it will ultimately be of no avail. Therefore, we reluctantly listen to it. We did not expect that, in addition to directly exploiting the people, you would turn to borrowing the name of the Central Government as a talisman and issuing tens of millions of public bonds in the form of raising funds. You are also people of Sichuan. Please search your conscience in the quiet of the night and think about the people of Sichuan who are on the verge of death today. What strength do they have to bear this heavy burden? Is it not caring about the lives and deaths of the people? Not only will there be soldiers without people, and no source of military pay, which is not fortunate for your army, but today, the red disaster is rampant, and everywhere is being poisoned by it. If it forces a popular uprising, like the irreparable situation in Jiangxi, how can you escape this heavy blame? Therefore, we cannot help but implore you to consider the suffering of the people and voluntarily withdraw the proposed issuance of public bonds. If you think that the military pay is insufficient, and it is difficult to do so, you may wish to consider the sluggishness of the entire Sichuan and slightly implement a policy of austerity. Or, you can temporarily inject the savings you have accumulated from extortion in the past to allow the people to escape the disaster this year, and then compensate them in the future when they have the strength. It is not impossible. If you must use the two words "post-war affairs" as an excuse, regardless of everything, and insist on plucking all the melons on the Huangtai Melon Vine, then even if the public bonds are issued in the future, there will still be no way to do good afterwards. What face will you have to see the elders of Jiangdong? Not to mention the resentment of the people. Therefore, our association does not avoid offense and sincerely petitions for the people. In a moment of urgency and desperation, we do not choose fine words and speak to each other with tears streaming down our faces. If you also believe that our colleagues are acting out of conscience and do not find loyal advice unpleasant to hear, then please show your respect for our homeland and leave a glimmer of hope for the 70 million people. Not only will our association colleagues be deeply grateful, but we will also send a telegram to inform you. We respectfully hope that you will take it into consideration. These are just some words. The matter concerns the vital interests of 70 million people in Sichuan. Whether directly or indirectly, inside or outside Sichuan, everyone is greatly affected. We hope that everyone will uphold their conscience and work together to liberate themselves, and unanimously request the central government to reject it and urge the two Liu authorities to cancel the proposed plan, unite compatriots inside and outside the province, and oppose it to the death. Do not stop until the goal is achieved. What can we do in the face of the great disaster in the future? Our association is a part of the people of Sichuan and dares not lag behind in loving our homeland and saving it from disaster. We only seek to benefit our elders, and we would not hesitate to do anything to serve them, even if it means wearing out our bodies. However, our strength is weak, and we are afraid that it will not be effective. We cannot help but hope that all parties will pursue and remember the past and work together to overcome difficulties. We respectfully send a telegram to inform you. Please consider it. Sichuan Native Place Association in Shanghai." [Stamped] "Issued from the office at No. 15, Jiujiang Road, Shanghai."

Request to Exempt Completed Consolidated Tax from Business Tax 132

Joint Chamber of Commerce Sends Telegram to Central Government

The Shanghai Joint Chamber of Commerce sent a telegram to the Executive Yuan and Legislative Yuan in Nanjing, stating: "To the Executive Yuan and Legislative Yuan of the National Government in Nanjing: The Business Tax Law passed by the 145th session of the Legislative Yuan has been promulgated by the National Government. Article 1 states: 'The business tax is a local income. All businesses operating in the cities of each province and the Executive Yuan shall pay business tax, except for factories that pay factory tax to the central government or banks organized as joint-stock companies that pay income tax.' This is clearly to implement a one-tax-per-item system to eliminate the harsh policies of repeated taxation during the likin era. According to the law, the factories mentioned naturally include a group of factories that manufacture goods. For example, cotton textile factories that have completed the consolidated tax on cotton yarn or cotton fabrics directly woven from it, when the goods are moved from the factory to the warehouse for storage, and then from the warehouse to the sales outlet set up by the factory for business, although the goods are moved to three different places, the main body and behavior of the business are still one. The warehouses for storing goods and the sales outlets for selling goods belonging to the factory are all included in the word 'factory' and should be excluded together with the factory. There should be no reason to levy business tax again. However, the officials in various provinces who collect business tax are mostly filled by personnel from the former likin agencies, and they inevitably still hold the views of the likin era. They often distort the clauses, resulting in repeated taxation of one item. The members of our association only know that one tax per item is the principle of the government's tax policy, and they believe that the repeated levying of this business tax is contrary to the original intention of the legislation. Although they have repeatedly and earnestly stated their views, they have not been corrected. The future of national products is chilling. The members are deeply concerned and have successively arrived at the association to request that the central government be requested to recognize that the word 'factory' in the above clauses should be considered to include the warehouses for storing goods and the sales outlets for selling goods belonging to the factory as the same commercial entity and the same business behavior. Issue an order to exempt this repeated business tax in order to relieve the difficulties of merchants and benefit tax revenue. We are extremely eager to await orders." Shanghai National Products Factory Joint Association, East.

Inspection Report of the Central Bank 136

94th Time

The 94th inspection report of the issuance reserve of the Central Bank states: "In accordance with the provisions of Article 15 of the Central Bank Ordinance, this council is responsible for inspecting the reserve funds for the issuance of convertible notes of the bank. On July 20, 1931, we conducted the 94th inspection at the bank's issuance bureau and hereby announce the inspection results as follows: (A) Total amount of convertible notes issued: 36,000,005,007 silver dollars, including 33,388,3675 silver dollar notes and 2,121,332 fractional currency notes. Total amount of reserve funds for convertible notes: 36,000,005,007 silver dollars, including 24,113,007 silver dollars in cash reserve. This cash reserve is counted as 16,851,410 yuan stored in the bank's issuance vault, 2,217,811 yuan stored in branches in various ports, and 5,043,786 yuan stored with fellow banks. The guarantee reserve is equivalent to 11,892,000 silver dollars. (B) Total amount of customs gold convertible notes issued: 1,000,000 yuan. Total amount of reserve funds for customs gold convertible notes: 1,000,000 yuan. This reserve fund includes 400,000 US dollars, stored with fellow banks in this port, at a fixed price of 40 customs gold. The above numbers are in accordance with Article 2 of the Central Bank's Convertible Note Regulations, which stipulates that 60% of the reserve must be in cash and 40% in guarantee. The results of this inspection show that the cash exceeds 60% and the guarantee is less than 40%, which is in compliance with the regulations. This report is hereby made." July 20, 1931, Chairman of the Supervisory Committee of the Central Bank, Li Fuxun, Supervisor Wang Jingli, Bei Songsun, Qin Runqing, Yu Qiaqing, Lin Kanghou, Xu Jifei.

Local News 2

Continued Trial of the "Snow Butterfly" Case 147

Sentencing Scheduled for 8:00 AM on the 11th

The case involving Hu Die, a female actress from the Star Film Company, and her former fiancé, Lin Xuehuai, regarding the termination of their engagement and the recovery of debts, is being litigated in the Special District Local Court. After two hearings by the Special Court, the case was postponed for three months due to the need to investigate evidence. Once the investigation procedures were completed, both parties were notified, and witnesses were subpoenaed. The hearing was scheduled to continue yesterday morning. Since the case has always been of public concern, after the date of the hearing was announced, those who wanted to witness it firsthand gathered at the Special Court at 8:00 AM yesterday morning. Initially, many lingered in the square or inquired at various courtrooms, not knowing where the trial would be held. Men and women crowded together, sweating profusely, but did not mind the hardship, finding it enjoyable instead. It was not until 9:30 AM, when the plaintiff Hu Die and her father, Hu Shaogong, arrived at the court with their representative lawyer, Zhan Jifeng, and went straight to the first courtroom on the third floor, that the crowd realized that the trial would be held there. They immediately swarmed upstairs. At that time, the criminal case in the courtroom had not yet been completed, but the people entering the courtroom continued to pour in, and the noise was particularly loud. The bailiffs stopped them, and order was barely maintained. It was already 10:00 AM when Judge Zhou finished hearing the criminal case and left the courtroom. Soon after, Judge Zhou Daren, who was presiding over the "Snow Butterfly" case, took the bench and first inquired about the subpoenaed witnesses. Only Zhou Jianyun, the business director of the Star Film Company, had arrived. Although Hu Die had previously stated that Anfei Garage and Zhao Huisan were at 49 Avenue Albert in the French Concession, the Special Court sent officials to serve subpoenas, but they could not be found. Therefore, no one arrived yesterday. The defendant, Lin Xuehuai, did not arrive until Judge Zhou took the bench. He was accompanied by his defense lawyers, Eson and Ni Zhengyao. Lin was wearing a flannel suit and sat in the back row of the lawyer's seats. Hu was wearing a white dress with red flowers and sat in the witness stand.

The gazes of the two met, but they seemed to be worlds apart. Judge Zhou then ordered Hu Die to stand in the witness box and asked her to point out the money Lin Xuehuai had borrowed from the check stubs that had been obtained from the Industrial and Commercial Bank. Hu carefully examined each stub and marked with a pencil those that were given to Lin with the character "Lin." There were six stubs in total, amounting to 199 yuan and 2 jiao and 73 taels of silver. Judge Zhou then gave the stubs to Lin to read and asked if he admitted to borrowing the money. According to Lin, although he had borrowed the money by check, he had repaid it one day after it was due. If the plaintiff had indeed lent him the money, she would have a ledger to prove it. He hoped that she would produce the ledger so that they could settle the account. As for the price of the car, he had also repaid it. Lawyer Eson presented the car registration certificate donated to the French Concession. Since Lin denied owing the money, the judge asked Hu Die how she could prove it. Hu stated that, for example, the money for Tang Rongxiang was actually

The price of the suit that Lin paid. As for other debts, at the time, because of their relationship as relatives, it was inconvenient to ask for receipts. Now, he knows that my company has been destroyed by fire and the ledger has been burned, so he is using the ledger as a condition to demand it. The judge then asked if she could not terminate the engagement. Hu replied that the matter had already reached this point, and there was no reason not to terminate the engagement. If they did not terminate the engagement, they would have to get married in the future, and it could be said with certainty that there would be no good outcome. At this point, the judge summoned the witness Zhou Jianyun to inquire about his age and occupation. After he made an affirmation, he testified truthfully. Zhou said that he had known Lin for seven or eight years and Hu for only three or four years. Lin used to be an actor at Star Film Company, and Hu is currently an actress at Star Film Company. I participated when Lin and Hu got engaged. Later, Lin only acted in one film and then left Star Film Company, so they did not often interact. I feel that this pair of

Fiancés had a very good relationship. However, between the autumn and winter of last year, I heard rumors that both sides were dissatisfied. I happened to talk to Hu about it, and Hu expressed her dissatisfaction, saying that Lin was squandering the money she gave him and dancing with other people. I was deeply concerned that their marriage would encounter obstacles, so I advised them as a friend, hoping that they would reconcile. However, although Hu expressed her dissatisfaction, she did not reveal any intention to terminate the engagement. Later, I met Lin, and Lin said that he could not completely trust the reports in the tabloids about Hu's actions, but he could not ignore them either. The two sides became suspicious of each other, which led to the current situation. As for the 600 yuan that Ms. Hu borrowed from Star Film Company, Hu said that it was for Lin

To use for his gold business. Later, when I asked Lin about this, he also denied it. The purchase of the car was also what Hu told people, saying that the price of the car was paid by her. However, Lin did not admit it later. The judge then summoned Lin to ask who initiated the termination of the engagement. Lin still said that it was from Hu, saying that on November 18th of last year, he went to meet with Zhou after Zhou Jianyun summoned him by letter. Zhou told him that Hu had gone to the company with her father and sisters to ask for assistance in terminating the engagement. I asked Zhou to persuade her. The next day, I visited Zhou again, and he said that Hu's intention was firm and could not be reversed. After I (Da Bao) published the news that Hu's behavior was improper and her reputation was tarnished, I tried to persuade her every time I saw her, until after November 15th, when I stopped seeing her. I also sent a letter on November 28th proposing to terminate the engagement. The judge then asked Hu Die what

Were the reasons for requesting the termination of the engagement? Hu said that she had already stated them in her complaint. If we consider the current situation, it is even more difficult to maintain the engagement. The defendant's desire to maintain the engagement is nothing more than to avoid repaying the debt and compensating for the loss. However, since the defendant proposed to terminate the engagement first and clearly stated in the letter that they would break off all relations, how can the engagement be maintained? As for the debt of 185 yuan, 191 taels of silver, the loan of 1,385 yuan, the loan of 600 yuan borrowed from Star Film Company, and the car, which should be returned at the price of 380 taels of silver, in addition to which, a loss of 1,000 yuan should be compensated. This loss is because of the three years of engagement, and he suddenly broke the engagement,

Causing time to be wasted and causing great mental suffering, which should be adequately compensated. Lin then stated that the plaintiff should provide reasons for requesting the termination of the engagement; otherwise, he would not agree. As for the various amounts being pursued, Lin still claimed that they had already been repaid. The judge then ordered the debate to begin. First, the plaintiff's lawyer, Zhan Jifeng, spoke, dividing his statement into two parts: (1) The part about terminating the engagement, stating that the dispute arose because the defendant arbitrarily squandered the plaintiff's money at the dance hall. The plaintiff and her father witnessed and advised him against this, but the defendant became angry and wrote a letter to the plaintiff, proposing to terminate the engagement. The plaintiff still left room for negotiation, replying that she would only accept the proposal under certain conditions. However, the defendant's desire to terminate the engagement was urgent, and he continued to urge her in subsequent letters. This shows that

The defendant took the initiative to terminate the engagement, and the responsibility naturally lies with the defendant. Furthermore, there is another matter that proves this, that is, on the first day of the trial, the defendant published a counterclaim in the newspaper, stating that he wanted to terminate the engagement. Although the counterclaim has not yet been filed, his determination to terminate the engagement has already been exposed. According to Article 976 of the Family Law of the Civil Code, if a major event occurs, one can request the termination of the engagement. The defendant's previous actions can be considered a major event. Therefore, the plaintiff filed a lawsuit to terminate the engagement and, in accordance with the same law, the non-negligent party can demand compensation for damages from the negligent party. The negligence in this case lies with the defendant, who should naturally be ordered to compensate for the considerable losses in order to compensate the plaintiff

For the mental suffering she endured. (2) As for the debt, Lawyer Zhan stated the reasons for pursuing each amount one by one and requested that the defendant be ordered to repay them all, as well as the statutory interest and litigation costs from the date of the lawsuit until the end of the execution, which should also be borne by the defendant. Next, the defendant's lawyers, Eson and Ni Zhengyao, stood up to respond, first stating that Lin was the owner of a morning tea shop,

And not a jobless person. Next, they said that the plaintiff could only claim for the termination of the engagement and the losses from the termination, as well as the 600 yuan borrowed from Star Film Company, etc. As for the other debts, since the money belonged to Hu Die's company, her father should sue as the plaintiff. Since he did not have his father's legal authorization, he should be rejected according to the law. Finally, they debated the three items that the plaintiff could claim and said that the defendant's letter proposing to terminate the engagement was merely an invitation to offer. Since it was not agreed to by the plaintiff at the time, the letter had already lost its validity and he was not responsible for anything. As for

The losses claimed by the plaintiff, since there was no proof and the evidence for the 600 yuan was insufficient, they should be rejected. Judge Zhou then summoned Hu Shaogong to ask who opened Hu Die's company. Hu said that it was opened jointly by him and his daughter. The father and daughter had also discussed pursuing the debt before filing the lawsuit jointly. The defendant's lawyer then made another defense, and Judge Zhou announced that the debate was over and that the sentencing would be scheduled for 8:00 AM on July 11th.

Li Hongzhang's Great-Granddaughter Files Lawsuit for Inheritance 148

Accuses her Uncle and Brother

Requests Division of 750,000 Taels

The case of Li Jiaheng, the great-granddaughter of the late Qing Dynasty Minister Li Hongzhang, suing her husband for discord in the Special District Court, has been reported in this newspaper many times. Recently, she filed a lawsuit for property division. Yesterday was the date of the trial for Li Jiaheng's request that her uncle, Li Mugong, and her brother, Li Jiasu, divide the inheritance. Li Jiaheng arrived in court with her lawyer, while Li Jiasu and Li Mugong claimed to be ill and did not arrive. Their lawyers appeared in court on their behalf. The meaning of her complaint is that she is requesting to divide her late father's inheritance. The 181st Central Political Conference of the National Government resolved that women's inheritance rights should be re-evaluated, and women, whether married or unmarried, should have equal inheritance rights with men. Also, according to Article 1 of the Implementing Rules for Retroactive Inheritance of Property by Married Women, the resolution on the effective date of the new interpretation of women's inheritance rights stipulates that for property inheritance that began after the following dates, even married women have inheritance rights: (1) The date on which the resolution on the women's movement of the Second National Congress was notified to all provinces by the former Judicial Administration Commission in October of the 15th year of the Republic of China; (2) For provinces that were not yet under the National Government on the date of the notification, the date on which they came under its jurisdiction. Jiangsu Province came under the jurisdiction of the National Government in the 16th year of the Republic of China. Jiaheng's late father, Guojun, inherited property from his father and ancestors, owning approximately 3 million taels worth of fields and houses, which he shared with the defendant Li Mugong, who was his biological brother. On April 23rd of the 18th year of the Republic of China, Jiaheng's father passed away. His death was the date on which Jiaheng's inheritance began. The notification arrived before, and Jiaheng's inheritance began after, so Jiaheng certainly has the right to inherit property according to the law. Jiaheng has already entrusted lawyers such as Ge Zhaoji to send a letter to the defendant, requesting a division. The defendant has acknowledged all the property owned by the defendant in a letter of acknowledgment. Since the defendant acknowledged but did not actually implement the division, Jiaheng only has the right to resort to litigation to request a division. The court must approve the division, and so on. Judge Zhou Daren ascended the seventh civil court and first had Li Jiaheng testify. Since she disagreed with her husband, Zhang Jinjiang, and left home last year, she now lives alone on Avenue Aierjin. The marital issues have already been brought up in the divorce lawsuit in your court. However, her late father, Li Guojun, unfortunately passed away on April 23rd of the 18th year, and all the savings she should have received have not been given to her. After marrying Zhang, he did nothing and had no family property, so his clothing and food were all supplied by my family. Her father promised her a dowry of 20,000 yuan when he was dying, but it is still with her stepmother. All the jewelry and other items from her wedding have been used for daily household expenses, and she is now empty-handed. Even the court fees cannot be paid immediately, as can be imagined from her circumstances. She and Jiasu are biological siblings, and Mugong is her uncle. When her father was alive, all the family's property was managed by her uncle. Her family's assets total 3 million taels, including foreign houses at 1, 2, and 4 Xin Chongqing Road, the land rights to which are jointly owned, worth approximately 1 million yuan. When Taiping Bank opened, her uncle wanted to serve as a director, so he requested that her father deposit 100,000 yuan in cash, with 50,000 yuan deposited in Mugong's name. After her father's death, the money was still managed by her uncle. Other public stocks were worth approximately several tens of thousands of yuan. The property in Suzhou was worth approximately tens of thousands of yuan. There is a property behind the Nanjing Police Department, which was where her father's concubine lived when he was alive. After her father's death, it was also managed by Mugong. There are still 40,000 dan of rice in her hometown, and other items are worth approximately 3 million taels. Her father was the second eldest, and he and Mugong were the only siblings. Her father had Jiasu and her, and there were two deceased elder sisters. She should receive a portion of her father's share, calculated as one-quarter, which amounts to 750,000 taels. When her father was dying, he had an oral will, but no written will. Today, the defendant's lawyer claims that there is a will that can be proven, which she does not understand. At this point in the interrogation, the plaintiff's lawyer stated that Li Jiaheng was ill when she came to court, so some of the property numbers she mentioned in court may have been omitted, and a separate list would be presented later. Because the defendant did not arrive, the court adjourned the case and scheduled another hearing.

Municipal Ferry Adds Night Service 150

Effective July 10th

The west side of Shanghai is bustling, and there is a lack of good places to escape the summer heat in the evenings. The municipal ferry, in view of this, has added a night service, going directly to Donggou and Gaoqiao in Pudong, selling only first-class and second-class tickets. The outbound ferry departs from the Shanghai Bronze Man Pier at 8:00 PM every night, arriving at Donggou at 8:50 PM and Gaoqiao at 9:30 PM. The inbound ferry departs from Gaoqiao at 11:00 PM, arriving at Donggou at 11:30 PM and the Bronze Man Pier at 12:00 AM. The one-way ticket price is one yuan for first class and five jiao for second class, and the round-trip ticket price is one yuan and five jiao for first class and eight jiao for second class. The service will be effective starting July 10th. After this, people on the sea can take the ferry for a trip on the river after dinner, enjoy the cool breeze, and appreciate the scenery. People who live on either side of the Huangpu River during the day can also take the ferry home in the cool of the evening, which is also a convenience.

Public Utilities Bureau Resolves Water Supply Dispute in Baoshan Lane, Zhabei 151

The Owner Closes the Water Gate

The Authorities Intervene

Baoshan Lane on Baotong Road, Zhabei, has 50 two-story buildings. Numbers 1 to 33 are owned by a Zhao family, and numbers 34 to 50 are rented out by the Zheng Shaode Hall. Recently, the Zheng family owner, citing excessive water fees, closed the main water pipe at the entrance of the lane throughout the day, except for 7:00 to 8:00 PM in the evening, allowing only a small amount of water to pass through. The residents felt inconvenienced and repeatedly negotiated without success, so they requested relief from the Municipal Public Utilities Bureau. The bureau sent staff to question the owner, but the owner did not admit to closing the water gate, instead claiming that there was insufficient water in Zhabei. Subsequently, the Zhabei Water and Electricity Company was ordered to investigate, and it was confirmed that the owner had closed the main switch of the lane. It was immediately opened, and the water flowed smoothly. The bureau also ordered the owner to fully supply water to the residents for drinking according to the regulations and not to close the water pipe arbitrarily, or face punishment.

A Record of Yesterday's Continued Trial in the Qu Case 152

Mundon Already Found Guilty After Interrogation

After the trial of the American soldier who committed the assault in the Qu case continued yesterday morning at the military court of the US Marine Corps Headquarters on Haifang Road, the part involving Corporal Mundon has been completed, and he has been found guilty. According to the law, he will be sentenced to imprisonment for a period of six months to twenty years. According to American military law, if the defendant is not guilty, he will be released immediately after the trial. If he is found guilty, the sentence will not be announced in court and will be announced after being submitted to a senior officer for approval. After Mundon's trial was completed yesterday, he was still sent back to custody, so although the sentence was not announced in court, it is already known that he is guilty. According to the charges against Mundon of intentionally, maliciously, and without justifiable reason stabbing Qu Ruixiang and Ma Chengbu, two Chinese tailors, Mundon admitted to using a knife, but claimed that he acted in self-defense. Therefore, when the defendant's testimony was taken yesterday, Mundon did not testify again. Only Major Krut of the US Marine Corps testified that Mundon's character was good in the camp, and Hall, the secretary of the Naval Youth Association, also testified. Now, his sentence will be submitted to the Commander-in-Chief of the US Asiatic Fleet for approval before being announced. The parts involving the two orderlies, Ginas and Daniel, will be tried separately next week.

Kissing and Traffic Problems

Outside the Westfield station in New Jersey, USA, is a very busy intersection. Every morning, between 8:15 and 8:22, the trains depart, and the workers come like a tide to catch the train to work in the city. Their wives or lovers often come along to give them a farewell kiss. This has caused great difficulty for the police officers directing traffic at the intersection. They reported to the police station that the kissing of thousands of people every day is obstructing traffic, causing many vehicles to stop to avoid them. Therefore, they suggested that the authorities should stipulate that each person should only kiss once, and leave immediately after kissing, without lingering. However, despite the report, there was ultimately no solution.

Ye Chuqiang's Leisurely Mood 154

— Li Qingduo

In the past, poets and scholars mostly loved wine, such as Li Bai, Bai Juyi, and other great masters, all of whom wrote poems about drinking wine, expressing elegance and timeless sentiments. Therefore, wine was a source of recreation for scholars. The newly appointed National Government Committee Member and Acting Chief Secretary Ye Chuqiang was originally a famous figure in Shanghai, with a background in journalism. His literary talent and moral character were highly praised at the time. Ye loved wine, and would always have a drink with his meals during his free time. Occasionally, at elegant banquets, amidst the bright lights and wine, he would raise his cup and enjoy the moon, his leisurely mood soaring. When the wine was half-finished, discussions would arise, bringing joy to the entire gathering, which was particularly refined. Ye often took a little fine wine before writing, then rested his head on the desk for a nap. After waking up from the tipsiness, his literary inspiration would be ignited, and he would create beautiful prose with a flourish of his pen, without hesitation, in one go. One day, the Minister of the Central Propaganda Department, Liu Luyin, hosted a banquet, and the Deputy Minister of the Central Organization Department, Zhang Daofan, and Ye Chuqiang were also present. During the conversation, they mentioned Ye's habit of drinking before writing, and all deeply admired Ye's elegance. During the banquet, Zhang jokingly said to Ye, "You are getting older, why not abstain from wine to maintain your health?" Ye smiled, indicating that it would be difficult to break away from wine for the time being. The elegance of a famous scholar and the profound interest of a refined person were widely admired in the capital at the time.

Anecdotes of Silas Hardoon 155

— Jing Mengdie

Silas Hardoon, a wealthy man in Shanghai, has passed away. The newspapers have detailed his family history and deeds. Here, I record a few anecdotes I heard in Wuxi as a separate biography.

Several years ago, Hardoon took his wife, Luo Jialing, to visit Wuxi and stayed in Mei Garden for half a month. They spent their days lingering at the Zhahe Pavilion and Tianxin Terrace, admiring the scenery. He once told the garden owner, Rong, that his love for this garden even surpassed that of the Aili Garden (Hardoon Garden in Shanghai). This is because Shanghai is prosperous, with bustling traffic and ten zhang (a Chinese unit of measurement, approximately 3.3 meters) of dust and noise, while this garden boasts the beauty of lakes and mountains, with a naturally tranquil and picturesque setting. The positions are different, and some things cannot be changed by money and power alone.

When Hardoon first arrived in Shanghai, he was merely a porter for a foreign firm. Later, he became wealthy by cooperating with the firm owner in land development and buying land. He benefited from the element of earth throughout his life. In the five elements, earth represents wealth. It is said that having earth means having wealth. Hardoon was fortunate to have the element of earth in his life, making him a living god of wealth. Luo was his companion during his humble beginnings. Fortunately, she had keen insight and could recognize a hero. She formed a bond of hardship with Hardoon and eventually became a divine couple.

Behind the Scenes of the Jiaotong University Graduation Ceremony 156

— Cheng Zhizheng

The National Jiaotong University has been established for 35 years. Nearly ten thousand graduates have served the community. The 31st graduation ceremony was held on the 2nd of this month. Representatives from the National Government, the Executive Yuan, the Ministry of Education, and the Ministry of Railways attended. The day before, there was also an exhibition of achievements and various farewell dinners, making it an unprecedented grand occasion for the university.

The Clever Metaphor of a Daughter Marrying　On the evening of the 30th, the president of the university held a farewell dinner for the graduating students. A banquet was held in the Wen Zhi Hall, attended by more than 200 guests and hosts. President Li Zhaohuan said in his speech that the graduation of the students was like a daughter marrying. They usually gathered together, but now they would be scattered to the ends of the earth. This made the parents (referring to the faculty and staff) reluctant to part. He hoped that they would often return to their parents' home to visit after marriage, and if they were dissatisfied, they should tell him so that he could try to find a solution. Dean Shi of Beiping hoped that the daughters would follow the principle of "obeying the husband rather than the parents" after marriage and serve their husbands in every way. He compared himself to an old nanny. Dean Zhong said that when the young ladies were working hard, they should not forget their original identities. They were "from famous families" and not ordinary girls. They should not only follow the old rules in railway construction but also improve them from time to time. His remarks were particularly clever and made people laugh heartily.

Mayor Zhang's Smiling Face　Mayor Zhang, the representative of the National Government, gave a sincere speech. He wore a white Zhongshan suit that day and spoke with a smiling face, hoping that the graduating students would not fail the government's painstaking efforts in cultivating talent. Then, Xu Juntao, the director of the Municipal Education Bureau and representative of the Executive Yuan, gave a speech, discussing various inventors such as Ford and Edison, citing them as examples to encourage the students.

Flower Baskets Piled in Front of the Podium　It is common practice for female schools to present flower baskets at graduation. However, this was the first time it had been seen at the graduation ceremony of Jiaotong University. This year, because three Misses graduated, many people presented flower baskets, which were colorful and piled in front of the podium, adding a lot of color to the auditorium. The university also considered this graduation of female students as an unprecedented event for Jiaotong University and specially issued diplomas separately to show their excellence.

Ma Yinchu's Humor　Ma Yinchu, the Chairman of the Economic Committee of the Legislative Yuan, is known for his humor. In his speech that day, he described the evils of society and how easily those who were new to it could be assimilated. His remarks were particularly profound. Ma said that in the past, there was an American student who returned to China and worked in an institution. According to the institution's rules, bonuses were distributed every year. In the first year, the student firmly refused to accept the bonus, believing it to be ill-gotten gains and should never be taken. In the second year, before the end of the year, he had already asked his colleagues when the bonus would be issued. In the third year, he went even further and paid for the bonus in advance. It can be seen that the environment changes people, which is alarming.

A Small Talk on the Willow Leaf Goby 157

— Lü Bing

The willow leaf goby is a small fish, but it is quite famous in Wuxing. The fish resembles the fork-tailed goby, but it is rounder and more plump, and its mouth is also more rounded. When cooked thoroughly with clear oil, the taste is not only delicious, but the flesh does not contain small bones, which is a special feature. The belly is full of eggs, which have a unique flavor. Therefore, when people in Huzhou buy willow leaf gobies, they always choose those with full breasts, presumably because the many eggs are enough for a good chew.

Willow leaf gobies are not often seen. They usually appear in groups during the fourth and fifth months of the lunar calendar when the rainy season begins and the streams rise. Wuxing is surrounded by mountains on all sides, and the accumulated rain flows horizontally and rushes down. At this time, the willow leaf gobies begin to come out in groups and swim upstream against the tide, scattering their eggs in the streams and lakes. Fishermen know their habits and usually set nets at the point where the water flows rapidly to wait. With one lift of the net, they can catch dozens. These lively little fish are caught and sold immediately, often being served on the table less than half an hour after being caught. Therefore, willow leaf gobies in Wuxing are never kept overnight. Even if fishermen occasionally cannot sell them all, they must return home to share them with their wives and children.

According to the villagers, a magistrate once came to govern Wuxing and did not recognize the willow leaf goby, thinking it was an ordinary fork-tailed goby. Later, his staff praised its beauty and cooked it for him to taste. The magistrate enjoyed it greatly, saying it was the best thing he had ever tasted, and asked why the willow leaf goby was so particularly delicious compared to other fish. The staff said that most fish swim downstream, but this fish uniquely swims upstream against the current. When the water flows against the current, the force is strong, and the fish willingly withstands the impact. It is said that it is tempered by the force of the water, which makes it develop more fully and deliciously than other fish. This theory is also reasonable, so I record it.

The season for willow leaf gobies in Wuxing is only a few weeks each year. The fish is best eaten immediately after cooking. It often spoils overnight. Therefore, it can be sealed in cans, which is suitable for other fish, but not for willow leaf gobies. I used to live in Wuxing and tasted its deliciousness. In recent years, I have been traveling far from home, and I have no fortune to enjoy the delicacies of my hometown. Writing this, I cannot help but drool.

Travel Notes from India (61) 158

— Linghua

On February 16th, I rode my bicycle from the Benares Hindu University to Sarnath, also known as Deer Park, where the Buddha first preached to the five monks. I have visited it several times, but not in detail. Today, I went to visit again. This place is about five or six miles from the city, which is about sixteen or seventeen Chinese miles. I went northwest out of the city, passing Victoria Park and crossing a clear river. There were fewer and fewer residents. When I reached a place, there was a sign saying "To Sarnath," so I turned northeast. According to the municipal and township governments, this sign is very important and should be written in large letters on the main roads to make it easier for pedestrians and save the trouble of asking for directions. On both sides of the road were small houses of residents, and the women all had red flowers pierced through their noses. The people were all very dark. From here, the car went north, and the road was flat and clean. Cars came and went, and the dense shade of the trees was very lovely. Going due north again, I arrived at Sarnath and saw the newly built Buddhist University. When I arrived, there were Burmese monks there. Two teachers and eight students were in class. A retired old gentleman was teaching English. The Burmese monk told me that he was a lawyer from Allahabad who had retired in his old age and wished to build a house here to spend his remaining years and enter Buddhism. In his spare time, he taught the young people science and kept many of his English and Indian books in the library. Several of his students had become famous, so he did not miss his home. I waited for him to finish class and invited him to talk under the trees outside. He had heard my lecture in Allahabad. Now, he was directing several servants to build a house and transport wood to live near the monks. This is because the Deer Park is open and spacious, with many trees and a small river, making it very suitable for building a house here. There are many rich people in China who do not know how to use their wealth to enjoy themselves. This old man is also awakened. India is peaceful everywhere. Building a house on the road and enjoying the mountains and rivers is enough to spend his life. The monks were very happy that I had come and offered me a glass of milk. When they have completed their studies in the future, they will all have to come east to China and Japan to revive Buddhism. When I am with the Indians, we all feel very close. They regard China as their own flesh and blood, and the Chinese also feel that India is their spiritual motherland. To the south of the university, there is a group of houses. I went to see it with the monks. They said it was the public place of the Nigrantha sect. The houses are solid, about a hundred or so, with residences inside. It is very unclean. It seems that the Nigrantha sect has not declined to this day. I saw their new temple in Calcutta, which was very magnificent. I asked the monks about the Nigrantha sect. They said that it is also considered a branch of Buddhism, but they are forbidden to wear clothes and practice naked, enduring the cold and heat without a thread, which is their characteristic. As for eating and drinking, they do not move their hands but are fed by others. I laughed when I heard this. There is nothing that does not exist in India. If this sect were to go to Siberia, how would they survive? A few dozen steps west of the Nigrantha public place, there is an Antiquities Museum, established by the British government. The trees are neat and tidy. When you enter it, many of the houses are closed. There are many things to see, such as stone Buddha statues. Many are beheaded and lack limbs. There are various Buddha statues, said to be the incarnations of the Buddha in past lives. If you calculate from this, there are countless kalpas in the past, and the various images of the Buddha can fill the whole world. I think that with the Buddha's wisdom, he must have known that stone statues are useless and superfluous, and he spoke of the merits of making statues to encourage all beings to happily make statues all over the world, using this to leave a memory for thousands of years in order to revitalize Buddhism. After all, this is the Buddha's wisdom, because he knew that everything is easily destroyed, but stone carvings are more permanent. However, everywhere, the heads and bodies are in different places, and the hands and feet are broken. The Buddha is helpless about karma. There are also statues of Krishna, etc., who are the leaders of Hinduism.

Short story by the Rotary Club

？？？(11) 159

— Xu Zhuodai

After resting for a while, Ziliang smelled a burnt smell in his nose. He thought to himself, what's burning?

He had to push open the window:

"What's that smell? Something's burning!"

No one answered downstairs, not even the nanny in the kitchen. How strange! Where have the two people downstairs gone? The burnt smell from the kitchen was rising straight up. Ziliang knew that the rice had been burnt. They must have suddenly left halfway through cooking, and the firewood in the stove didn't go out, so the rice was all burnt.

"Is anyone downstairs?"

Still no one answered. Ziliang thought, if it keeps burning, won't the pot burn through? He was worried, so he didn't care about his own affairs and hurried downstairs. He looked around the living room, but there was no one. When he looked at the kitchen, he saw that the back door was wide open. It turned out they had gone out the back door. Ziliang looked out the back door and saw that someone was clearing the sewer in the alley, with three or four people standing there watching. Sure enough! His virtuous wife and his precious nanny were also standing there watching. Ziliang was furious:

"What's so interesting about clearing the sewer? The rice is burning!"

He shouted loudly.

The two of them were startled and rushed back in through the back door. Ziliang followed behind. He saw the nanny had already taken out the burnt firewood. Yueru opened the pot lid and added water. Ziliang's anger hadn't completely subsided.

"You haven't seen clearing the sewer before? You don't even care that the rice is burning."

The wife was unwilling to show weakness:

"Now that the rice is burnt, you can come over and add some water and put out the fire. Why don't you do it yourself and instead run outside to make a fuss? Burnt rice makes a better porridge than anything else. Don't you know that?"

"You always say that as long as someone is willing to study, no matter how big or small, everything is knowledge. Then, isn't clearing the sewer a kind of knowledge?"

Ziliang thought, now that they were in the kitchen, it was none of his business. His own work was important. Once he decided this, he turned around and went upstairs.

Commercial News

Gold Standard Prices Ultimately Trend Downward 160

US Attitude Firm on War Debt Case

Total of 14.5 Taels Recalled Throughout the Day Yesterday, July 3rd, the gold exchange opened as usual. The gold standard trend was weak and the state was chaotic, fluctuating up and down. New York has always been the largest area for selling raw silk. Unexpectedly, since the summer, silk sales have not improved for a long time, and recently they have become stagnant. Local Chinese silk merchants sent telegrams to New York to inquire. The raw silk market has no factory sales, so the telegrams sent by Shanghai Chinese silk merchants have not been forwarded. Telegrams to Lyon and England silk have also rarely been forwarded to Shanghai. Yesterday, only Kaili imported 10 packages of Shanghai white factory silk, Xinfu imported 6 packages of Sichuan yellow factory silk, and Kechang imported 5 packages of yellow silk. However, the most important Zhenmei green tea market has become more and more quiet. Only the core-extracted goods had a slight outlet yesterday, and the rest had no transactions, it is said.

Piece Goods: Woolens Have Only Sporadic Transactions 175

The woolen goods business has been declining day by day. Various summer white goods, except for a slight embellishment from the Shanghai tailor shops on this street, have not been inquired about at all. Most of them are retail businesses involving cutting and selling piece by piece. White Biji, white Zhigong, feather yarn, barrel cloth, gauze twill, crepe cloth, yellow twill, etc., continue to be needed, but purchases are not large, because it is already late, and most people want to sell off their existing goods. Yesterday, Ningfeng silk's striped barrel cloth sold for three liang five qian and a half, while Susheng sold for three liang. Mitsui silk stripes sold for three liang six qian, white Biji for four liang, and white Zhigong for four liang five qian and a half.

Raw Cotton Yarn Sales Are Uniquely Strong in the Hot Weather 176

This Factory's Cotton Cloth: The market rose and then softened, because the overseas cotton market was sluggish, and the gold price was difficult to rise, so people's hearts were scattered. However, there is a severe shortage of spot goods for fine cloth, so it has not fallen. Yihua's Golden Three Pagodas bleached cloth is also firm, selling for nine liang six qian. Since the unbleached cloth wholesalers have united, the price of goods has been able to hold steady, especially the Blue Double Fish silk that refuses to loosen at all. The Ten Thousand Years Green fine cloth, which was temporarily out of stock, has gradually arrived in Shanghai, opening at nine liang. Among the coarse cloths, the 9-pound and 11-pound goods have slightly fallen, the 13-pound goods are stable, and the 16-pound goods are not as smooth as before. The sales of this factory's velvet cloth have also come to an end.

Eastern and Western Piece Goods: The overall market is slightly down, with the Eastern goods' Moonflower Velvet and Zhigong Ni being relatively soft. In fact, the July goods have gradually arrived in Shanghai, and since the gold market has fallen, the tax rates and pricing are smaller than before, so everyone wants to sell. Bleached cloth is also soft, with Magpie Bridge Meeting at twelve liang five qian and a half, the Three Cities at eleven liang nine qian, and Heavenly Gift Golden at ten liang four qian. Fushou Samsung is eleven liang one qian and a half. Only patterned cloth is still hard, regardless of light or dark colors and Luen Chang goods, all must be exported at five liang. Raw cotton yarn has been selling well due to the continuous hot weather, with forty or fifty pieces sold every day. Dian Qiuxiang is ten liang one qian, Little Beauty is eleven liang nine qian and a half, and Hanshan Temple is nine liang seven qian, it is said.

Hardware: English Tinplate Market Revives 177

Garden Lead Wire Arrives, Price Falls

English Tinplate: Since the foreign exchange rate has become loose, the standard has been affected first, and selling prices have fallen one after another, selling for only fifteen liang per box. In recent days, overseas pricing has increased, and local business has also been very active, so 800 or 900 boxes have been opened, and the market has recovered to fifteen liang four or five qian per box, and 100-pound goods have also risen to sixteen liang five qian, it is said.

Garden Lead Wire: Previously, due to a shortage of goods, the standard soared, rising to five liang and a half per bundle, so the general industry purchased from Japan. In recent days, goods have continued to arrive, and the Japanese exchange rate has also fallen, so the cost is low. Various industries have adopted the principle of selling off goods, so the market has declined, and each bundle is selling for only four liang seven qian and a half, it is said.

Miscellaneous News: 370 pieces of Huzhou silk were shipped to France.

2,000 pieces of Lanzi were shipped from Wuhu.

1,200 tons of steel bars and machinery were shipped from England to Shanghai.

1,300 pieces of cotton yarn and foreign cloth were shipped to Nanhua.

1,000 bags of green beans were shipped to India.

2,100 pieces of foreign paper were shipped from Japan.

1,300 pieces of American cotton arrived in Shanghai today.

50 pieces of Jinshan squid arrived yesterday, costing 78 liang.

Hakodate Telegram: The new kelp is still good this year, and it will be available on the market around the end of the month.

Correction: Yesterday's Silk and Tea (Haining New Local Silk Opening Prices Rise) was actually North-South Goods (Xin Zhengzhou Tea Has Arrived in Hankou). This is hereby corrected.

Social News

The Grievances of American "Editors and Publishers" 196

Gangster Movies and News are Harmful to Youth; The American People are Drowning in a Sea of Vulgar Literature.

The American magazine "Editors and Publishers" states that Paul Block published an editorial in various newspapers titled "Stop Gangster Movies." The president of the World Film Association, Mr. Lan Moore, replied in a letter, saying, "Why not instruct your newspaper reporters to stop publishing gangster news?" He also stated that he knows the activities of gangsters are indeed a kind of news material, and at the same time, they are also film material because they are an important part of world affairs. Therefore, they are bound to be shown in movies, just like being published in newspapers. He concluded by saying that he has never seen a film that rewards gangsters. According to the reporter's view, the way some newspapers, film companies, book publishers, and drama producers have handled crime news in the past five years should be widely criticized. Mr. Lan Moore may not have seen films that reward gangsters, but we have. The way some newspapers extravagantly narrate gangster news is equally harmful. It must be known that sensational robber behavior best suits the tastes of generally ignorant, idle, and passionate youth who are eager for love and indulgence in seeking pleasure. Although most films, books, dramas, and newspapers indicate that evil people are eventually arrested and reviled, the allure of an exciting life may not be restrained by the thought of prison. Therefore, all those who edit news and produce films should realize the importance of their responsibilities. All of life, whether good or bad, must be depicted according to its truth. If it is excessively described, given seductive colors, and then publicly performed, it will be greatly harmful to civilization. Today, the American people are already drifting in a sea of vulgar, inelegant, mixed, and impure literature and films. This kind of literature and film, under the name of realism, struts around arrogantly, looking down on everything. Even if we don't consider morality and civilization, but only for the sake of safe profit-seeking, we should not indulge this evil trend.

Fading Interest in Bullfighting in Spain 197

Madrid News: Spain has a traditional custom of bullfighting. The scene of bullfighting is extremely cruel. In recent years, under the vigorous opposition of animal protection societies, the general psychology has gradually changed, shifting their interest to beneficial sports such as tennis and football. Furthermore, animal protection societies have advocated the enactment of laws against animal cruelty. The former Duke of Alba gave his full support. Now, there has been great progress in laws concerning animal cruelty. Recently, two people were sued for abusing a dog, and the court sentenced them to fines and imprisonment according to the law. Public opinion in society has undergone a complete change.

The Wit of a Serbian Executioner 198

"I am not responsible for your death."

Belgrade News: Serbia used to execute criminals

Page 22

by shooting, but recently switched to hanging. The first person to be hanged was gendarme George Chifaje Vich, who was sentenced to death for murder. During the execution, the executioner wore a top hat and white gloves. After the execution was completed, he discarded his white gloves at the feet of the deceased and loudly shouted, "George Chifaje Vich, I am not responsible for your death."

The German Scientific Renaissance Movement in Secrecy 200

— Yao Qu

Recently, Mr. Wilen, Vice President of the American Astral Communication Society, returned from a German conference and stated that scientists in that country are secretly researching and inventing a rapid-fire aircraft that can cross the ocean in half an hour, hoping to realize this in the next two years. It is said that the operation of this aircraft relies entirely on liquid fuel, and its horsepower is greater than that of all current fuels. Now that liquid fuel has been invented, the fundamental problem has been solved, and the period of realization is only limited to the final improvement of the rapid-fire aircraft. Once this aircraft is put into practical use, it can carry 50 pounds of mail each time, making communication between Europe and the United States more convenient. In the future, by using this aircraft as a blueprint for gradual improvement, the ideal of lunar travel may be greatly realized within ten years. After this news spread, it was like a thunderclap, astonishing the American scientific community. No one expected that the Germans, in their silence, still had such far-sighted research.

Amidst this shock, news suddenly arrived that the Paris Morning Post's correspondent in Germany had been expelled because the correspondent secretly entered a laboratory, photographed instruments, and was discovered, immediately being deported. Although some say that the correspondent's actions were improper, the German's painstaking research and strict secrecy are evident here.

The American Scientist's Strange Theory: Don't Continent Sigh for the Moon Leaving as Its Son 201

San Francisco News: Green Shan Huang, present at the Gadge Gege Dr. Science Conference, published his research at the conference, stating that "The moon was once separated from the earth, and the part of the Pacific Ocean is where the moon came out. Like the land order of the American continent, a granite belt was discovered at a depth of twenty-five miles below. This land order is not the bottom of the Pacific Ocean, but the place where the continent continuously ends is the bottom of the ocean. Based on the experiment of the past two years, the earthquake in California originates from the Mojave Desert, eight miles deep in the Pacific Ocean. Most of the earthquakes in the Pacific Ocean originate from the thin land order taken by the moon. This is probably because the continent sighed for the moon leaving as its son." Also at the same conference, Mr. Feiya Lian published his research on the Sang Jia Sha Island earthquake, saying that "The moon's gravitational pull on the tide is related to earthquakes."

British Army Tank Strategy 202

Infantry-Based Strategy Presents a Major Change

London News: The British Army authorities believe that future battles will start with tanks, so the standing force uses four battalions of tank brigades, 200 tanks, equipped with full-wavelength radio and three 47-meter projectile guns. The tactics first involve sending three-ton light tanks to rush the battlefield, then dispatching super-heavy tanks to clean up the remaining enemy forces, coupled with attacks from the air and the organization of support squadrons, requisitioning civilian vehicles to transport troops. A major change is presented to the infantry-based strategy.

Social News Submission Guidelines 203

(1) Text should be about domestic and foreign science, industry, commerce, rural

(2) News on hygiene, aviation, exploration, customs or urban life is limited. Pictures are limited to various lyrical books about social life.

(3) Photos that are qualified are those related to seasons, scenery, flora, fauna, people, and news photography. Photos of ladies in seasonal scenery are especially welcome.

(4) Each text should not exceed 2,000 characters.

(5) Do not write on both sides of the manuscript paper.

Business News 204

Sincere Company declares: This company's exquisitely crafted Chinese and Western-style towels, gauze, and colorful bathrobes are of superior quality, beautiful design, suitable size, and bright colors. After a bath in fragrant water, wearing this robe will bring coolness and comfort, completely dispelling the sweltering heat.

Qing Lian Ge Shopping Center on Fourth Malu declares: Since this shopping center moved to the newly built mansion on Daxin Street, business has been thriving. Now, the owner of this place, in order to enhance the entertainment for distinguished guests, has opened a "Small Guanghan" on the third floor, gathering famous flowers from Beili to sing Beijing tunes and current songs. It is scheduled to be held day and night starting today. From 3:30 PM to 7:00 PM in the afternoon and from 8:30 PM to 12:00 AM in the evening, tea fees will not be increased as a courtesy. The popularity of tourists can be predicted.

Fushou Pharmacy at the intersection of Fourth Malu and Wangping Street declares: This store has newly released a No. 101 Cholera Prevention Pill, which has the effect of increasing the resistance of the stomach and intestines and preventing the invasion of germs. Taking it when sick can turn danger into safety. Now during the hot summer, it is specially sold at a low price for one month.

Theater News 205

Mingxing Company declares: The new film "Hong Lei Ying," which has been in production for a long time by this company, is directed by Zheng Zhengqiu after "Peach Blossom Lake." It stars Hu Die, Zheng Xiaoqiu, Xia Peizhen, and Xi Jianong. The plot tells a story of triangular love. The film is glamorous and beautiful, tortuous and novel, and quite thought-provoking. The layout is also very compact. The sets for the entire film are spared no expense, beautified everywhere, and grand and magnificent as never before. The cost is quite considerable. Now this film is 80-90% complete, and the completion date is imminent.

Shanghai Market Editorial Department Notice 206

(1) All businesses, doctors, film companies, theaters, and books

(2) When painters send manuscripts, please indicate "Shanghai Market Department Received." All businesses, film companies, theaters, painters, and doctors who send manuscripts should stamp them for proof; otherwise, they will not be published.

(3) The usual practice of paying a small fee for lengthy film manuscripts remains the same. It is calculated at one dollar per thousand words.
